-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f7ebbadae62b4546ad1df58a1471260a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f7ebbadae62b4546ad1df58a1471260a");'><span id='f7ebbadae62b4546ad1df58a1471260a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1145')">1141-1145年</a>，9-13岁</div><div id='f7ebbadae62b4546ad1df58a1471260a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年11月</a>　随父至长沙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1145')">1142-1145年</a>　侍亲家中。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6ed1817f961343ceab2ffdcc100a7ed0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6ed1817f961343ceab2ffdcc100a7ed0");'><span id='6ed1817f961343ceab2ffdcc100a7ed0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1167')">1165-1167年</a>，33-35岁</div><div id='6ed1817f961343ceab2ffdcc100a7ed0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　在长沙始与诸学友过从讲习。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　序胡宏《知言》作品：胡子知言序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《胡子知言序》篇末称“辄序遗书，贻于同志”，似乾道初年作，姑缀于此。）</span><div id='poem_1272687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>胡子知言序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272687")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272687'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272687'>《知言》，五峰胡先生之所著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272687_comment'></div>先生讳宏，字仁仲，文定公之季子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272687_comment'></div>自幼志于大道，尝见杨中立先生于京师，又从侯师圣先生于荆门，而卒传文定公之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272687_comment'></div>优游南山之下馀二十年，玩心神明，不舍昼夜，力行所知，亲切至到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272687_comment'></div>析太极精微之蕴，穷皇王制作之端，综事物于一源，贯古今于一息，指人欲之偏以见天理之全，即形而下者而发无声无臭之妙，使学者验端倪之不远，而造高深之无极，体用该备，可举而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272687_comment'></div>晚岁尝被召旨，不幸寝疾，不克造朝而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272687_comment'></div>是书乃其平日之所自著，其言约，其义精，诚道学之枢要，制治之蓍龟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272687_comment'></div>然先生之意，每自以为未足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272687_comment'></div>逮其疾革，犹时有所更定，盖未及脱稿而已启手足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272687_comment'></div>或问于某曰：「《论语》一书，未尝明言性，而子思《中庸》独于首章一言之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272687_comment'></div>至于孟子，始道性善，然其为说则已简矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272687_comment'></div>今先生是书于论性特详焉，无乃与圣贤之意异乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272687_comment'></div>某应之曰：无以异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272687_comment'></div>夫子虽未尝指言性，而子贡盖尝识之，曰：「夫子之文章可得而闻也，夫子之言性与天道不可得而闻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272687_comment'></div>是岂真不可得而闻哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272687_comment'></div>盖夫子之文章无非性与天道之流行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272687_comment'></div>至孟子之时，如杨朱、墨翟、告子之徒，异说并兴，孟子惧学者之惑而莫知所止也，于是指示大本而极言之，盖有不得已焉耳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272687_comment'></div>又况今之异端直自以为识心见性，其说诪张雄诞，又非当时之比，故高明之士往往乐闻而喜趋之，一溺其间，则丧其本心，万事隳弛，毫釐之差，霄壤之缪，其祸盖有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272687_comment'></div>先生于此又乌得而忘言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272687_comment'></div>故其言有曰：「诚成天下之性，性立天下之有，情效天下之动」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272687_comment'></div>而必继之曰：「心妙性情之德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272687_comment'></div>又曰：「诚者，命之道乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272687_comment'></div>中者，性之道乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272687_comment'></div>仁者，心之道乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272687_comment'></div>而必继之曰：「惟仁者为能尽性至命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272687_comment'></div>学者诚能因其言而精察于视听言动之间，卓然知夫心之所以为妙，则性命之理盖可默识，而先生之意所以不异于古人者，亦可得而言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272687_comment'></div>若乃不得其意而徒诵其言，不知求仁而坐谈性命，则几何其不流于异端之归乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272687_comment'></div>某顷获登门，道义之诲，浃洽于中，自惟不敏，有负夙知，辄序遗书，贻于同志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272687_comment'></div>不韪之罪，所不得而辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272687_comment'></div>门人广汉张栻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1272687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年1月18日</a>　编成《二程粹言》，并作序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年10月</a>　校订刘珙所刻《二程先生文集》，并与、刘珙、朱熹讨论校正《二程先生文集》误字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年10月</a>　取父手泽与太原陈伯雄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年11月</a>　时往重修后的岳麓书院讲学，论《大学》次第，示学者以公私义利之辨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　馆杨万里于南轩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　撰成《诸葛忠武侯传》<div id='poem_1272753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉丞相诸葛忠武侯传跋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272753")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272753'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272753'>广汉郡张栻曰：三代衰，五伯起，而功利之说盈天下，谋国者不复知正义明道之为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272753_comment'></div>三老董公独得宏纲，以告汉高帝，惜高帝犹未能尽其用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272753_comment'></div>武侯当汉祚之季，乃能执其机而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272753_comment'></div>其言曰：「汉贼不两立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272753_comment'></div>臣鞠躬尽力，死而后已，至于成败利钝，非臣之明所能逆睹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272753_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272753_comment'></div>此夏少康四十年经营宗祀，而卒以配天之本心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272753_comment'></div>若侯者可谓有正大之体矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272753_comment'></div>自幼读书，独观大略，晨夜从容，抱膝长啸，其胸中所见，岂浅识所能窥哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272753_comment'></div>高卧隆中，不求闻达，盖将终身焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272753_comment'></div>昭烈，汉室之胄也，而三顾之于草庐，名义既正，好贤之意又笃，安得不以身许之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272753_comment'></div>昭烈与侯相周旋，一以道义而忘势，受遗之际，君臣肝胆相照，无纤芥形迹，何其盛也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272753_comment'></div>侯恢复规摹，先务为根本之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272753_comment'></div>方建兴初，务农训兵，内治国事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272753_comment'></div>国事既定，北向致讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272753_comment'></div>军旅将发，拳拳之忧实在后主，拜表纳忠，反复曲折，专以宫中府中之事为言，且陈亲贤臣、远小人之义，荐郭攸之等使在左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272753_comment'></div>一篇之中，三四致意焉，而其终章尤为切至，侯之虑抑深且远矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272753_comment'></div>即侯行事而观之，绝姑息之私意，本常理之大公，如明镜洞然四达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272753_comment'></div>其闻过惟恐不及，见善若出诸己，用人各尽其器能，至或有罪，虽入幕上宾如马谡，流涕斩之而弗释也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272753_comment'></div>故李平、廖立既被废放，没齿怀德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272753_comment'></div>盖侯于斯世所欲不存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272753_comment'></div>娶妇沔南，惟贤是取，人之讪笑不复顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272753_comment'></div>身都将相三十年间，家之所有仅足子弟衣食之奉，及其既没，内无馀帛，外无赢财，视天下无一足以动乎中者，其正大之体岂不具哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272753_comment'></div>侯之事后主小心恭恪，一国之柄举出其手，而人不知其为权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272753_comment'></div>彼怀奸稔逆、窃窃窥人宗祀者，雨雪见睍而谓侯敌哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272753_comment'></div>侯之规摹，至使耕者杂于渭滨，而军无私焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272753_comment'></div>舆图之复，已恢恢然在目中矣，不幸薨谢，匪大数然欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272753_comment'></div>或谓侯劝昭烈取荆州为不义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272753_comment'></div>不知刘琮既已迎降于操，则荆州固魏之荆州矣，于以取之，岂不正乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272753_comment'></div>惜昭烈之失此机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272753_comment'></div>又或谓魏延之策惜侯不用，不知夫天将昌汉，以侯之举措扫禽乱贼直馀事耳，行险侥倖，非侯志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272753_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272753_comment'></div>秦汉以来，士狃于战国之馀习，张子房为拔出者，而犹未免乎杂以伯术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272753_comment'></div>若侯真豪杰之士，无文王犹兴者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272753_comment'></div>然使侯得游于洙泗之门，讲学以终之，则其所至，又非予所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272753_comment'></div>予每恨陈寿私且陋，凡侯经略次第，与夫烛微消患、治国用人、驭军行师之要，悉闇而不章，幸杂见于他传及裴松之所注，因裒而集之，不敢饰辞以忘其实，其妄载非实者则删之，庶几读者可以得侯之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1272753_comment'></div>近世钜公作史书，编年乃以魏年号接汉献之统，故其所书名不正而言不顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1272753_comment'></div>予谓献帝虽废，而昭烈以正义立于蜀，武侯辅之，汉统未坠地也，要尽后主末年始系魏年号为正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1272753_comment'></div>始侯在隆中，传称以管、乐自许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1272753_comment'></div>予谓侯盖师慕王者之佐，其步趍则然，岂与管、乐同在功利之域者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1272753_comment'></div>意其传者之误，故不复云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1272753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1272753'><span class='label'>按：</span>《汉丞相诸葛忠武侯传》卷末，四部丛刊续编本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1272753_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年1月</a>　《经世纪年》脱稿。作品：经世纪年序。<div id='poem_1272680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>经世纪年序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272680")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272680'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272680'>太史迁作《十二国世表》，始记甲子起于成周共和庚申之岁，庚申而上则莫纪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272680_comment'></div>历世寖远，其事杂见于诸书，靡适折衷，则亦传疑而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272680_comment'></div>本朝嘉祐中，康节邵先生雍出于河南，穷往知来，精极于数，作《皇极经世书》，上稽唐尧受命甲辰之元，为《编年谱》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272680_comment'></div>如去外丙、仲壬之祀，康节以数推知之，乃合于《尚书》成汤既没太甲元年之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272680_comment'></div>因康节之谱，编自尧甲辰至皇上乾道改元之岁，凡三千五百二十有二年，命之曰《经世纪年》，以便观览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272680_comment'></div>间有鄙见，则因而明之，如孟子谓尧、舜三年之丧毕，舜、禹避尧、舜之子而天下归之，然后践天子位，此乃帝王奉天命之大旨，其可闇而弗章？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272680_comment'></div>故皆书其服丧践位之实焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272680_comment'></div>夏后相二十有八载，寒浞弑相，明年，少康始生于有仍氏，凡四十年而后祀夏配天，不失旧物，故于此四十载独书少康出处，而纪元载于复国之岁，以见少康之君臣经营宗祀，绝而复续，足以为万代之冠冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272680_comment'></div>于新莽之篡，缺而不书，盖吕氏不可间汉统，而所假立惠帝子亦不得而纪元，故独以称制书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272680_comment'></div>以至周文王之称王，武王之不纪元于国，皆汉儒传习之缪，先觉君子辨之详矣，故皆正而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272680_comment'></div>汉献之末，曹丕虽称帝，而昭烈以正义立于蜀，诸葛亮相之，则汉统乌得为绝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272680_comment'></div>故献帝之后，即系昭烈年号，书曰蜀汉，逮后主亡国，而始系魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272680_comment'></div>凡此皆节目之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272680_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272680_comment'></div>世有古今，而古今不间于一息，事有万变，而万变卒归于一原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272680_comment'></div>盖理义根乎天命而存乎人心者，不可没也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272680_comment'></div>是故《易》本太极，《春秋》书元，以著其体用，其示后世至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272680_comment'></div>然则大《易》、《春秋》之义，其可以不明乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272680_comment'></div>乾道三年正月甲子谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1272680_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年2月</a>　有书致朱熹，担心近习为恶。作品：答朱元晦秘书书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年9月8日</a>　与朱熹相见论学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年10月</a>　为张孝祥作《敬简堂记》<div id='poem_1272838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敬简堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272838")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272838'>历阳张侯安国治长沙，既踰时，狱市清净，庭无留民，以其閒暇辟堂，为燕息之所，而名以「敬简」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272838_comment'></div>他日与客落之，顾谓某曰：「仆之名堂，盖自比于昔人起居之有戒也，子其为我敷畅厥义」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272838_comment'></div>某谢不敏，一再不获命，因诵所闻而言曰：「圣贤论为政，不曰才力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272838_comment'></div>盖事物之来，其端无穷，而人之才力虽极其大，终有限量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272838_comment'></div>以有限量应无穷，恐未免反为之役，而有所不给也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272838_comment'></div>君子于此抑有要矣，其惟敬乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272838_comment'></div>盖心宰事物，而敬者心之道所以生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272838_comment'></div>生则万理森然，而万事之纲总摄于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272838_comment'></div>凡至乎吾前者，吾则因其然而酬酢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272838_comment'></div>故动虽微，而吾固经纬乎古之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272838_comment'></div>事虽大，而吾处之若起居饮食之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272838_comment'></div>虽杂然并陈，而釐分缕析，条理不紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272838_comment'></div>无他，其纲既立，如鉴之形物，各止其分而不与之俱往也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272838_comment'></div>此所谓居敬而行简者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272838_comment'></div>若不知举其纲而徒简之务，将见失生于所怠，而患起于所忽，乃所以为纷然多事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272838_comment'></div>故先觉君子谓饰私智以为奇，非敬也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272838_comment'></div>简细故以自崇，非敬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272838_comment'></div>非敬则是心不存，而万事乖析矣，可不畏欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272838_comment'></div>虽然，若何而能敬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272838_comment'></div>克其所以害敬者，则敬立矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272838_comment'></div>害敬者莫甚于人欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272838_comment'></div>自容貌颜色辞气之间而察之，天理人欲丝毫之分耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272838_comment'></div>遏止其欲而顺保其理，则敬在其中，引而达之，扩而充之，则将有常而日新，日新而无穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272838_comment'></div>侯英迈不群，固已为当世之望，诚能夙夜警励，以进乎此，则康济之业可大，而岂特藩翰之最哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272838_comment'></div>侯曰：「然则请书以为记，以无忘子之言」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1272838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1272838'><span class='label'>按：</span>《南轩集》卷一二。又见《于湖居士文集》附录，光绪《湖南通志》卷三二，民国《简阳县志》诗文存五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1272838_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　与张孝祥、朱熹登定王台，有诗酬唱。作品：十三日晨起霜晴用定王台韵赋此。<div id='poem_113118' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113118' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113118?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十三日晨起霜晴用定王台韵赋此</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113118")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_113118_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113118'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113118'>晴岚开岳镇，云雨断阳台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113118'>日出寒光迥，川平秀色回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113118'>兴随天际雁，诗寄岭头梅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113118'>盛事它年说，凭君记玉杯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113118'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_113118_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　与张孝祥、朱熹登赫曦台，联句。作品：登岳麓赫曦台联句。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月6日</a>　与朱熹、林用中自潭城渡湘水，登衡山。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b3d8473594ca45878394ec2e60cc891c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b3d8473594ca45878394ec2e60cc891c");'><span id='b3d8473594ca45878394ec2e60cc891c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1169')">1168-1169年</a>，36-37岁</div><div id='b3d8473594ca45878394ec2e60cc891c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年6月</a>　过访陈符溪亭。作品：陪舍人兄过陈仲思溪亭深有买山卜邻之意舍人兄预以颛壑见名因成古诗赠仲思。<div id='poem_113370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113370' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113370?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪舍人兄过陈仲思溪亭深有买山卜邻之意舍人兄预以颛壑见名因成古诗赠仲思</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113370")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_113370_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113370'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113370'>筑居湘水滨，岁月亦已久。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113370'>宁知负郭东，胜处入君手。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113370'>回环烟坞深，有此溪十亩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113370'>朝暾穿林薄，荷气薰户牖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113370'>堂堂吾州牧，下马唤宾友。<div id='poem_sentence_4_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_113370'>主人故喜事，一笑具殽蔌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_113370'>汲泉泛崇莲，洗盏倾稚酒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_113370'>淋漓壁间书，自可传不朽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_113370'>我独留薄莫，并溪时矫首。<div id='poem_sentence_8_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_113370'>人言君不偶，此岂落人后。<div id='poem_sentence_9_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_113370'>观君眉宇间，似亦挟所有。<div id='poem_sentence_10_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_113370'>隔溪更幽绝，古木荫高阜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_113370'>却立望遥岑，四序列钟卣<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作卤，据康熙本、四库本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_113370'>买山吾计决，便欲剪榛莠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_113370'>居然颛一壑，岂羡印如斗。<div id='poem_sentence_14_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_113370'>未知邻家翁，还肯见容否。<div id='poem_sentence_15_113370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_113370'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_113370_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年8月</a>　送张孝祥作牧荆州。作品：送张荆州序。<div id='poem_1272672' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272672' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272672?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张荆州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272672")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272672_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272672'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272672'>客问于某曰：「张荆州之行，子将何以告之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272672_comment'></div>某应之曰：「吾将告之以讲学」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272672_comment'></div>客笑曰：「若是哉，吾子之迂也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272672_comment'></div>荆州早岁发策大廷，天子亲擢为第一，盛名满天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272672_comment'></div>入司帝制，出典藩翰，议论风采，文章政事，卓然绝人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272672_comment'></div>上流重地，暂兹往牧，所以寄任之意甚重，而天下士亦莫不引领以当世功名属于公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272672_comment'></div>夫以位达而名章，任重而望隆，吾子顾以讲学告之，不亦迂乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272672_comment'></div>某曰：「子以吾所谓讲学者果何也邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272672_comment'></div>盖天下之患莫大于自足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272672_comment'></div>自足则画矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272672_comment'></div>信如子言，荆州若挟是数者以居，则仆尚何道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272672_comment'></div>惟荆州方且退然若诸生，曾无一毫见于颜面，此仆之所以叹息慕向，而讲学之说是以敢发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272672_comment'></div>盖天下之物众矣，纷沦轇轕，日更于前，可喜可怒，可慕可愕，所以荡耳目而动心志者何可以数计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272672_comment'></div>而吾以藐然之身当之，知诱于外，一失其所止，则迁于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272672_comment'></div>夫人者，统役万物者也，而顾乃为物役，其可乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272672_comment'></div>是以贵于讲学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272672_comment'></div>天下之事变亦不一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272672_comment'></div>几微之形，节奏之会，毫发呼吸之间，得失利害有霄壤之势，吾朝夕与之接，一有所滞塞，则昧几而失节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272672_comment'></div>其发也不审，则其应也必盭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272672_comment'></div>一事之隳，万事之所由隳也，岂不可惧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272672_comment'></div>是以贵夫讲学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272672_comment'></div>夫惟讲学而明理，则执天下之物不固，而应天下之变不胶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272672_comment'></div>吾于天下之物无所恶，而物无以累我，皆为吾役者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272672_comment'></div>吾于天下之事无所厌，而事无以汩我，皆吾心之妙用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272672_comment'></div>岂不有馀裕乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272672_comment'></div>又岂有穷极乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272672_comment'></div>然所谓讲学者，宁有它求哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272672_comment'></div>致其知而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272672_comment'></div>知者吾所固有也，本之六经以发其蕴，泛观千载以极其变，即事即物，身亲格之，超然会夫大宗，则德进业广，有其地矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272672_comment'></div>夫然，故富贵不能淫，贫贱不能移，威武不能屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272672_comment'></div>居天下之广居，行天下之大道，致君泽民，真古所谓大臣者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272672_comment'></div>然则学其可忽乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272672_comment'></div>《诗》云：『如切如磋，如琢如磨』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272672_comment'></div>此之谓也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272672_comment'></div>某既以此告客，于荆州之别也，遂书以为献。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1272672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1272672'><span class='label'>按：</span>《南轩集》卷一五。又见《于湖居士集》附录，民国《简阳县志》诗文存五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1272672_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　为魏掞之作《艮斋铭》<div id='poem_1272856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272856?labeling=true' target='_blank'>艮斋铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272856")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272856_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272856'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272856'>艮斋，建安魏元履燕居之室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272856_comment'></div>在《易》，艮为止，止其所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272856_comment'></div>某尝考《大学》始终之序，以知止为始，得其所止为终，而知止则有道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272856_comment'></div>《易》与《大学》，其义一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272856_comment'></div>敬为之铭：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1272856'>物之感人，其端无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272856_comment'></div>人为物诱，欲动乎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272856_comment'></div>不能反躬，殆灭天理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272856_comment'></div>圣昭厥猷，在知所止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272856_comment'></div>天心粹然，道义俱全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272856_comment'></div>是曰至善，万化之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272856_comment'></div>人所固存，曷自违之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272856_comment'></div>求之有道，夫何远而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272856_comment'></div>四端之著，我则察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272856_comment'></div>岂惟虑思，躬以达之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272856_comment'></div>工深力到，大体可明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272856_comment'></div>匪由外铄，如春发生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272856_comment'></div>知既至矣，必由其知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272856_comment'></div>造次克念，战兢自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272856_comment'></div>事物虽众，各循其则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272856_comment'></div>其则匪它，吾性之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272856_comment'></div>动静以时，光明笃实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272856_comment'></div>艮止之妙，于斯为得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272856_comment'></div>任重道远，时不我留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272856_comment'></div>嗟我同志，勉哉勿休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272856_comment'></div>繄我小子，惧弗克力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272856_comment'></div>咨尔同志，以起以掖。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1272856_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　收到朱熹论学之信。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年2月</a>　上表谢恩。作品：谢太师加赠表。<div id='poem_1272406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢太师加赠表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272406")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272406'>日月昭回，烛孤忠于既没；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272406_comment'></div>风雷鼓动，诏恤典于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272406_comment'></div>藐然遗孤，重于陨涕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272406_comment'></div>伏念先臣早趋列著，即值多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272406_comment'></div>痛陵庙之莫扶，叹簪绅之自保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272406_comment'></div>以为寇雠若此，岂臣子之遑安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272406_comment'></div>义理所存，何利害之足计！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272406_comment'></div>会真人之勃起，先百辟以骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272406_comment'></div>奉命于危机汹涌之秋，投躯于众难纷纭之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272406_comment'></div>以至进登揆路，尽护戎车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272406_comment'></div>不忧丑虏之方张，惟惧人心之不正，炳若丹青之誓，率兹缟素之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272406_comment'></div>虽蒙神圣之深知，亦致奸邪之横疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272406_comment'></div>摈居炎服，中逾二纪之更；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272406_comment'></div>敢意馀龄，复际重明之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272406_comment'></div>窃窥睿蕴，思复祖疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272406_comment'></div>愿毕效于精诚，冀平清于氛祲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272406_comment'></div>而割地奉雠之论起，合党缔交之谋深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272406_comment'></div>修边备则指为费财，讲武功则目为生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272406_comment'></div>妄拟偷安于岁月，曾微却顾于兴衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272406_comment'></div>非惟沮先臣之为，实乃伤陛下之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272406_comment'></div>铄金成市，卒赖保全；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272406_comment'></div>易箦馀哀，空存感慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272406_comment'></div>怅历时之寖久，忽当馈以兴思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272406_comment'></div>中旨显颁，褒章具举，既极上公之贵，复稽节惠之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272406_comment'></div>人知忠义之荣，莫不竞劝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272406_comment'></div>士喜是非之定，少缓私忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272406_comment'></div>固将垂训于邦家，岂但增光于泉壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272406_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下勤俭法禹，聪明继尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272406_comment'></div>纬武经文，不暂忘于宗祏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272406_comment'></div>彰善瘅恶，用允若于天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272406_comment'></div>敷扬旧勋，表厉在服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272406_comment'></div>诵温言之曲尽，仰至意之旁孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272406_comment'></div>臣猥以承家，极兹追往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272406_comment'></div>奉牲以告，知神理之来歆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272406_comment'></div>聚族而谋，念上恩之曷报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272406_comment'></div>惟慕先臣之许国，力图后日之捐身。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1272406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　认同朱熹之悟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　收到朱熹论学之信。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　作《书明道先生遗文后》，授教授何蕴，刻于长沙府学。<div id='poem_1272758' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272758' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272758?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书明道先生遗文后</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道五年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272758")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272758_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272758'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272758'>右明道先生遗文九篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272758_comment'></div>长沙学宫既刻二先生文集，后三年，新安朱熹复以此寄栻，云得之玉山汪应辰，敬以授教授何蕴，俾嗣刻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272758_comment'></div>乾道己丑四月朔，广汉张栻谨书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1272758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1272758'><span class='label'>按：</span>《二程集》附录，中华书局一九八一年校点本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1272758_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　饯张枃于湘中馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　除知抚州，未上，改严州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='fd59c4f55b134f27bb56a572253c959d_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1174')">1171-1174年</a>，39-42岁</div><div id='fd59c4f55b134f27bb56a572253c959d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年12月</a>　抵长沙旧庐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　作《洙泗言仁序》<div id='poem_1272684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洙泗言仁序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272684")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272684'>昔者夫子讲道洙泗，示人以求仁之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272684_comment'></div>盖仁者天地之心，天地之心而存乎人，所谓仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272684_comment'></div>人惟蔽于有己，而不能以推，失其所以为人之道，故学必贵于求仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272684_comment'></div>自孟子没，寥寥千有馀载间，《论语》一书家藏人诵，而真知其旨归者何人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272684_comment'></div>至本朝伊洛二程子始得其传，其论仁亦异乎秦汉以下诸儒之说矣，学者所当尽心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272684_comment'></div>某读程子之书，其间教门人取圣贤言仁处类聚以观而体认之，因裒《鲁论》所载，疏程子之说于下，而推以己见，题曰《洙泗言仁》，与同志者共讲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272684_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272684_comment'></div>仁虽难言，然圣人教人求仁，具有本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272684_comment'></div>譬如饮食乃能知味，故先其难而后其获，所以为仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272684_comment'></div>而难莫难于克己也，学者要当立志尚友，讲论问辩于其所谓难者，勉而勿舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272684_comment'></div>及其久也，私欲浸消，天理益明，则其所造将有不可胜穷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272684_comment'></div>若不惟躬行实践之务，而怀蕲获之心，起速成之意，徒欲以聪明揣度于语言求解，则失其传为愈甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272684_comment'></div>故愚愿与同志者共讲之，庶几不迷其大方焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1272684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　作《主一箴》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　与吕祖谦论存养省察之功。作品：寄吕伯恭书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　秋，闻弟张枃自桂林归，喜而赋诗。作品：喜闻定叟弟归。<div id='poem_113221' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113221' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113221?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜闻定叟弟归</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113221")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_113221_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113221'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113221'>吾弟三年别，归舟半月程。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113221_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113221'>瘦肥应似旧，欢喜定<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>如兄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113221_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113221'>秋日联鸿影，凉窗听雨声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113221_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113221'>人间团聚乐，身外总云轻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113221_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113221'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_113221_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年1月10日</a>　偕许及之登卷云亭，望岳麓积雪，分韵赋诗。作品：长沙历冬无雪正月十日与客登卷云亭望西山始见一白莫夜复大作竹声萧然是日坐上分韵得云字。<div id='poem_113261' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113261' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113261?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长沙历冬无雪正月十日与客登卷云亭望西山始见一白莫夜复大作竹声萧然是日坐上分韵得云字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年1月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113261")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_113261_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113261'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113261'>冬温气苦盭，玄冥未书勋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113261'>薄雪殿馀腊，一夜收楚氛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113261'>欢欣想农圃，润泽到蒿芹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113261'>我亦破晓出，唤客来卷云。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113261'>苍苍西山树，栖此万鹤群。<div id='poem_sentence_4_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_113261'>爽气入病眼，幽怀惬前闻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_113261'>意到自举酒，语多祇论文。<div id='poem_sentence_6_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_113261'>薄莫势未已，飞花复缤纷。<div id='poem_sentence_7_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_113261'>还将萧瑟声，一一付竹君。<div id='poem_sentence_8_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_113261'>洗盏且更酌，清绝未酣醺。<div id='poem_sentence_9_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_113261'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_113261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_113261'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_113261_0'>⑴ 原作气，据缪刻本、康熙本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_113261_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　裒集《系辞说》作品：答陈平甫别纸。<div id='poem_1272581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答陈平甫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272581")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272581'>某自幼侍亲来南，周旋三十馀年间，又且伏守坟墓于衡山之下，是以虽为蜀人，而不获与蜀之士处，以亲友其仁贤，每以是念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272581_comment'></div>往岁得建安魏元履书，始知足下之名，且闻廷对所陈大略，念足下天资刚毅人也，恨未之识耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272581_comment'></div>虽然，世固有天资之美者，苟不知进乎学，则终身安于其故而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272581_comment'></div>盖气质虽美而有限，天理至微而难明，是以君子必贵乎学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272581_comment'></div>近得犹子然书，复闻足下超然拔出流俗，志于古道，孜孜不舍，则又叹足下于世衰道微之际，能独见自立如此，其进也何可量！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272581_comment'></div>则愿见之心益廑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272581_comment'></div>今得足下书并所论著，连缄累牍，伏而读之，无非以讨论问学为事，而果有以知足下之所存，甚幸甚惠！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272581_comment'></div>惟是不以仆为不敏，意欲与之共讲斯道，而勉为君子之归，固所愿者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272581_comment'></div>若夫推予期待之过，其实则非所敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272581_comment'></div>仆自惟念，妄意于斯道有年矣，始时闻五峰胡先生之名，见其话言而心服之，时时以书质疑求益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272581_comment'></div>辛巳之岁，方获拜之于文定公书堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272581_comment'></div>先生顾其愚而诲之，所以长善救失，盖有在言语之外者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272581_comment'></div>然仅得一再见耳，而先生没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272581_comment'></div>自尔以来，仆亦困于忧患，幸存视息于先庐，䌷绎旧闻，反之吾身，寖识义理之所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272581_comment'></div>湘中二三学者时过讲论，又有同志之友自远而至，有可乐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272581_comment'></div>如是又五载，而上命为州，不得辞，继为尚书郎，猥以戆言，误被简遇，遂得执经入侍，且须都省下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272581_comment'></div>诚欲自竭，庶几以报，而学力不充，迄亡毫发之补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272581_comment'></div>归来惟自省厉，盖愈觉己偏之难矫，圣学之无穷，而存察之不可斯须忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272581_comment'></div>诵《伐木》「神之听之，终和且平」之章，思欲与海内贤士切磋琢磨，庶几卒以无负初志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272581_comment'></div>然则自治之不暇，又乌能有益于人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272581_comment'></div>念辱足下万里盛意，则亦不敢隐耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272581_comment'></div>盖道之不明久矣，自河南二程先生始得其传于千有馀载之下，今二先生之言虽行于世，然识其真者或寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272581_comment'></div>夫二先生之言，凡以明孔、孟之道而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272581_comment'></div>孔、孟之道，其博厚高明，虽曰配二仪之无疆，然其端岂远于人心而欲它求哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272581_comment'></div>人病不能推而充之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272581_comment'></div>世之闻二先生之言而惊疑窃怪者固不足道，而其间有慕高远者，则又惝恍虚矜而不循其实，亦为失其真而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272581_comment'></div>窃考二先生所以教学者，不越于居敬、穷理二事，取其书反复观之，则可以见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272581_comment'></div>盖居敬有力，则其所穷者益精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272581_comment'></div>穷理寖明，则其所居者益有地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272581_comment'></div>二者盖互相发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272581_comment'></div>为仁之要，孰尚于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272581_comment'></div>学而不知其要，则泛滥而无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272581_comment'></div>二者言之虽近，而意味工夫无穷，其间曲折精微，惟能用力者当渐知之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272581_comment'></div>升高自下，陟遐自迩，务本循序而进，久自有所至，不可先起求成之心，起求成之心，则有害于天理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272581_comment'></div>孔子之所谓获，孟子之所谓正者，政此病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272581_comment'></div>区区诵其所闻，言不尽意，惟愿足下毋忽于卑近以卒至于远大，则幸甚幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1272581_comment'></div>别纸所谕，亦各以鄙意批呈，未知然否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1272581_comment'></div>自尔既定交于万里之外，则不惜时惠音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1272581_comment'></div>有箴有诲、有得有疑，一一详及，勿为无益之书，所愿望也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1272581_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　辟岳麓书院，教授后学，钞有《南轩书说》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　与朱熹诘难释疑。作品：与朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　改定自撰《仁说》<div id='poem_1272789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272789?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仁说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272789")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272789'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272789'>人之性，仁、义、礼、智四德具焉：其爱之理则仁也，宜之理则义也，让之理则礼也，知之理则智也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272789_comment'></div>是四者虽未形见，而其理固根于此，则体实具于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272789_comment'></div>性之中只有是四者，万善皆管乎是焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272789_comment'></div>而所谓爱之理者，是乃天地生物之心，而其所由生者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272789_comment'></div>故仁为四德之长，而又可以兼能焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272789_comment'></div>惟性之中有是四者，故其发见于情，则为恻隐、羞恶、是非、辞让之端，而所谓恻隐者亦未尝不贯通焉，此性情之所以为体用，而心之道则主乎性情者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272789_comment'></div>人惟己私蔽之，以失其性之理而为不仁，甚至于为忮为忍，岂人之情也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272789_comment'></div>其陷溺者深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272789_comment'></div>是以为仁莫要乎克己，己私既克，则廓然大公，而其爱之理素具于性者无所蔽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272789_comment'></div>爱之理无所蔽，则与天地万物血脉贯通，而其用亦无不周矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272789_comment'></div>故指爱以名仁则迷其体<span class='inlineComment2'>（程子所谓爱是情，仁是性谓此。）</span>，而爱之理则仁也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272789_comment'></div>指公以为仁则失其真<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，而公者人之所以能仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272789_comment'></div>夫静而仁、义、礼、智之体具，动而恻隐、羞恶、辞让、是非之端达，其名义位置固不容相夺伦，然而惟仁者为能推之而得其宜，是义之所存者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272789_comment'></div>惟仁者为能恭让而有节，是礼之所存者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272789_comment'></div>惟仁者为能知觉而不昧，是智之所存者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272789_comment'></div>此可见其兼能而贯通者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272789_comment'></div>是以孟子于仁，统言之曰「仁，人心也」，亦犹在《易》乾、坤四德而统言乾元、坤元也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272789_comment'></div>然则学者其可不以求仁为要，而为仁其可不以克己为道乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1272789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1272789'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_1272789_0'>⑴ 程子所谓仁道难名，惟公近之，不可便指公为仁谓此。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1272789_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　撰《书说》，以《酒诰说》寄示朱熹。<div id='poem_1272800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酒诰说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272800")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272800'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272800'>酒之为物，本以奉祭祀、供宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272800_comment'></div>此即天之降命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272800_comment'></div>而人以酒之故，至于失德丧身，即天之降威也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272800_comment'></div>释氏本恶天降威者，乃并与天之降命者去之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272800_comment'></div>吾儒则不然，去其降威者而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272800_comment'></div>降威者天，而天之降命者自在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272800_comment'></div>为饮食而至于暴殄天物，释氏恶之，而必欲食蔬茹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272800_comment'></div>吾儒则不至于暴殄而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272800_comment'></div>衣服而至于穷极奢侈，释氏恶之，必欲衣坏色之衣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272800_comment'></div>吾儒则去奢侈而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272800_comment'></div>至于恶淫慝而绝夫妇，吾儒则去其淫慝而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272800_comment'></div>释氏本恶人欲，并与天理之公者而去之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272800_comment'></div>吾儒去人欲，所谓天理者昭然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272800_comment'></div>譬如水焉，释氏恶其泥沙之浊，而窒之以土，不知土既窒，则无水可饮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272800_comment'></div>吾儒不然，澄其沙泥，而水之澄清者可酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272800_comment'></div>此儒释之分也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1272800_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　改易《言仁录》诸说，寄吕祖谦《言仁录》一册。作品：寄吕伯恭书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　改易《言仁录》诸说，寄朱熹《言仁录》一册。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　撰《诗说》作品：与吴晦叔书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年8月</a>　重订《希颜录》作品：跋希颜录。<div id='poem_1272708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋希颜录</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道元年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272708")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272708'>某己卯之岁，尝裒集颜子言行为《希颜录》上下篇，今十有四年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272708_comment'></div>回视旧编，去取伦次多所未善，而往往为朋友所传写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272708_comment'></div>于是复加考究，定著为一卷，又附录一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272708_comment'></div>盖颜子之事，独载于《论语》、《易》、《中庸》、《孟子》之书，其间颜子之所自言，与夫见于问答者抑鲜矣，特圣人之所称及，曾子、孟子之所推述者，其详盖可以究知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272708_comment'></div>自孟子之后，儒者亦知所尊仰矣，而识其然者则或寡焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272708_comment'></div>逮夫本朝，濂溪周先生、横渠张先生出，始能明其心，而二程先生则又尽发其大全，于是孔子之所以授于颜子、颜子之所以学乎孔子，与学者之所当从事乎颜子者，深切著明，而无隐于来世者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272708_comment'></div>故今所录，本诸《论语》、《易》、《中庸》、《孟子》所载，而参之以二程先生之论，以及于濂溪、横渠与夫二先生门人高弟之说，列为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272708_comment'></div>又采《家语》所载颜子之言有近是者，与夫扬子云《法言》者，并史之所纪者，存之于后，盖亦曰学者之所当知而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272708_comment'></div>既已缮写，则抚而叹曰：嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272708_comment'></div>颜子之所至亚于圣人，孔门高弟莫得而班焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272708_comment'></div>及考《鲁论》，师友之所称有曰「不迁怒、不贰过」而已，有曰「以能问于不能，以多问于寡，有若无，实若虚，犯而不校」而已，自学者观之，疑若近而易识，然而颜子之所以为善学圣人者实在乎此，则圣门之学，其大略亦可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272708_comment'></div>惟实用其力而后知其难，知其难而后有可进之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272708_comment'></div>然则后之学者贪高慕远，不循其本者，终何所得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272708_comment'></div>故予愿与同志之士以颜子为准的，致知力行，趋实务本，不忽于卑近，不遗于细微，持以缜密，而养以悠久，庶乎有以自进于圣人之门墙，是录之所为作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272708_comment'></div>乾道元年八月九日谨书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1272708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年9月</a>　为石𡼖作传心阁铭。作品：南剑州尤溪县学传心阁铭。<div id='poem_1272863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南剑州尤溪县学传心阁铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272863")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272863'>乾道九年，知南剑州尤溪县事石𡼖既新其县之学，复建阁于学之东北，买书五千卷藏之其上，而命工人绘濂溪周先生、河南二程先生之像寘于其中，使学者得共朝夕瞻仰焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272863_comment'></div>新安朱熹为之名曰传心之阁，而𡼖又以书请铭于广汉张某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272863_comment'></div>某窃惟念自孟子没，圣学失传，历世久远，其间儒者非不知尊孔孟而诵六经，至考其所得，则不越于诂训文义之间而已，于圣人之心，所以本诸天地而措诸天下与来世者，盖鲜克涉其藩，而况睹其大全者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272863_comment'></div>惟三先生生乎千载之后，乃能考诸遗经，而得其不传之妙以相授受，然后六经之言，群圣之心，全体大用，晦而复明，如日之中，万目皆睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272863_comment'></div>呜呼盛矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272863_comment'></div>某愚不敏，夙向往焉，敢以建阁之意、命名之说，洗心拜手，叙而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272863_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1272863'>惟民之生，厥有彝性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272863_comment'></div>情动物迁，以隳厥命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272863_comment'></div>惟圣有作，合乎天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272863_comment'></div>修道立教，以觉来今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272863_comment'></div>孰谓道远，始卒具陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272863_comment'></div>俾尔由学，而圣可成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272863_comment'></div>邹鲁云邈，章句有师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272863_comment'></div>一经皓首，语道则迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272863_comment'></div>惟子周子，崛起千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272863_comment'></div>熟探其源，以识其大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272863_comment'></div>立象尽意，阐幽明微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272863_comment'></div>圣学有传，不曰在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272863_comment'></div>惟二程子，实嗣其徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272863_comment'></div>既自得之，又光大之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272863_comment'></div>有浑其全，则无不总。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272863_comment'></div>有析其精，则无不中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272863_comment'></div>曰体曰用，著察不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272863_comment'></div>曰隐曰显，莫间其几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272863_comment'></div>于皇圣心，如日有融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272863_comment'></div>于赫心传，来者所宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272863_comment'></div>有屹斯阁，尤溪之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272863_comment'></div>翼翼三子，绘事孔明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272863_comment'></div>俨然其秋，温然其春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272863_comment'></div>揭名传心，诏尔后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272863_comment'></div>咨尔后人，来拜于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272863_comment'></div>起敬起慕，永思其传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272863_comment'></div>于味其言，于考其为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272863_comment'></div>体于尔躬，以会其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272863_comment'></div>尔之体矣，循其至而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272863_comment'></div>尔之至矣，道岂异而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1272863_comment'></div>传心之名，千古不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1272863_comment'></div>咨尔后人，无替厥初。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1272863_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　撰成《论语说》作品：论语说序。<div id='poem_1272683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论语说序</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道九年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272683")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272683'>学者，学乎孔子者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272683_comment'></div>《论语》之书，孔子之言行莫详焉，所当终身尽心者，宜莫先乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272683_comment'></div>圣人之道至矣，而其所以教人者大略则亦可睹焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272683_comment'></div>盖自始学则教之以为弟、为子之职，其品章条贯，不过于声气容色之间，洒扫应对进退之事，此虽为人事之始，然所谓天道之至赜者，初亦不外乎是，圣人无隐乎尔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272683_comment'></div>故自始学则有致知力行之地，而极其终则有非思勉之所能及者，亦贵于行著习察，尽其道而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272683_comment'></div>孔子曰：「道之不行也，我知之矣，知者过之，愚者不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272683_comment'></div>道之不明也，我知之矣，贤者过之，不肖者不及也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272683_comment'></div>秦汉以来，学者失其传，其间虽或有志于力行，而其知不明，擿埴索途，莫适所依，以卒背于中庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272683_comment'></div>本朝河南君子始以穷理居敬之方开示学者，使之有所循求，以入尧舜之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272683_comment'></div>于是道学之传，复明于千载之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272683_comment'></div>然近岁以来，学者又失其旨，曰吾惟求所谓知而已，而于躬行则忽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272683_comment'></div>故其所知特出于臆度之见，而无以有诸其躬，识者盖忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272683_comment'></div>此特未知致知力行互相发之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272683_comment'></div>孔子曰：「学而不思则罔，思而不学则殆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272683_comment'></div>历考圣贤之意，盖欲使学者于此二端兼致其力，始则据其所知而行之，行之力则知愈进，知之深则行愈达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272683_comment'></div>是知常在先，而行未尝不随之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272683_comment'></div>知有精粗，必由粗以及精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272683_comment'></div>行有始终，必自始以及终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272683_comment'></div>内外交正，本末不遗，条理如此，而后可以言无弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272683_comment'></div>然则声气容色之间，洒扫应对进退之事，乃致知力行之原也，其可舍是而它求乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272683_comment'></div>顾某何足以与明斯道，辄因河南馀论，推以己见，辑《论语说》，为同志者切磋之资，而又以此序冠于篇首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272683_comment'></div>乾道九年五月壬辰朔，广汉张栻序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1272683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　撰成《孟子说稿》作品：孟子讲义序。<div id='poem_1272685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孟子讲义序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272685")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272685'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272685'>学者潜心孔孟，必得其门而入，愚以为莫先于义利之辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272685_comment'></div>盖圣学无所为而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272685_comment'></div>无所为而然者，命之所以不已，性之所以不偏，而教之所以无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272685_comment'></div>凡有所为而然者，皆人欲之私，而非天理之所存，此义利之分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272685_comment'></div>自未尝省察者言之，终日之间鲜不为利矣，非特名位货殖而后为利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272685_comment'></div>斯须之顷，意之所向，一涉于有所为，虽有浅深之不同，而其徇己自私则一而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272685_comment'></div>如孟子所谓内交要誉、恶其声之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272685_comment'></div>是心日滋，则善端遏塞，欲迩圣贤之门墙以求自得，岂非却行以望及前人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272685_comment'></div>使谈高说妙，不过渺茫臆度，譬犹无根之木，无本之水，其何益乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272685_comment'></div>学者当立志以为先，持敬以为本，而精察于动静之间，毫釐之差，审其为霄壤之判，则有以用吾力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272685_comment'></div>学然后知不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272685_comment'></div>平时未觉吾利欲之多也，灼然有见于义利之辨，将日救过不暇，由是而不舍，则趣益深，理益明，而不可以已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272685_comment'></div>孔子曰：「古之学者为己，今之学者为人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272685_comment'></div>为人者无适而非利，为己者无适而非义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272685_comment'></div>曰利，虽在己之事，亦为人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272685_comment'></div>曰义，则施诸人者，亦莫非为己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272685_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272685_comment'></div>义利之辨大矣，岂特学者治己之所当先，施之天下国家一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272685_comment'></div>王者所以建立邦本，垂裕无疆，以义故也，而伯者所以陷溺人心，贻毒后世，以利故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272685_comment'></div>孟子当战国横流之时，发挥天理，遏止人欲，深切著明，拨乱反正之大纲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272685_comment'></div>其微辞奥义，备载七篇之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272685_comment'></div>如某者虽曰服膺，而学力未充，何足以窥究万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272685_comment'></div>试以所见与诸君共讲之，愿无忽深思焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1272685_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月</a>　作诗送弟张枃之官严州。作品：别离情所钟十二章四句送定叟弟之官严陵。<div id='poem_113306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别离情所钟十二章章四句送定叟弟之官严陵<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113306")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_113306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113306'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113306'>别离情所钟，会合意无斁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113306_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113306'>如何仅踰岁，复赋弟行役。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113306_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113306'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_113306_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_112949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_112949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/112949?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_112949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_112949'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_112949'>岁律亦已暮，风烈雪漫漫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_112949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_112949'>去路阻且长，念子衣裘单。<div id='poem_sentence_1_112949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_112949'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_112949_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_112947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_112947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/112947?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_112947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_112947'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_112947'>严之水沦漪，其山复苍苍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_112947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_112947'>子陵钓游地，草木有馀光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_112947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_112947'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_112947_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_112948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_112948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/112948?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_112948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_112948'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_112948'>我昔临此州，民容拙使君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_112948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_112948'>子行为多谢，慰彼无毫分。<div id='poem_sentence_1_112948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_112948'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_112948_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_113308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113308?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_113308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113308'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113308'>别驾亦何事，休戚理则同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113308'>但使民受惠，无论别驾功。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113308'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_113308_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_113310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113310?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_113310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113310'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113310'>巍巍孤高亭，念我昔所喟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113310'>子也时一登，千载起立志<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113310'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_113310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_113310'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_113310_0'>⑴ 自注：某在严陵，尝为宋广平立孤高亭。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_113310_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_113309' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113309' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113309?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_113309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113309'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113309'>义路本如砥，利径剧羊肠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113309'>何以书子绅，世德不可忘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113309'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_113309_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_113307' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113307' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113307?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_113307_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113307'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113307'>自昔谨交际，人情易因循。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113307'>敬始以念终，君子贵守身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113307'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_113307_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_112945' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_112945' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/112945?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_112945_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_112945'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_112945'>邻邦吕正字，质疑时以书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_112945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_112945'>校官有袁子，苦语莫厌渠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_112945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_112945'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_112945_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_112946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_112946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/112946?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_112946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_112946'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_112946'>藐兹遗体重，相对子与予。<div id='poem_sentence_0_112946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_112946'>祝子以自爱，念不忝厥初。<div id='poem_sentence_1_112946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_112946'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_112946_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_113311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113311?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_113311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113311'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113311'>云满南阳陌，书藏善和宅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113311'>行行重回首，无使归思隔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113311'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_113311_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_113312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113312?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_113312_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113312'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113312'>送子目力短，朔风吹我裾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113312'>心焉独如结，子也当念予。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113312'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_113312_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　春，积寒成疾，病势极危。作品：寄吕伯恭书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　病后往城南结小茅斋读书。作品：与朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　夏，改正《论语说》作品：与吴晦叔书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年9月</a>　建成城南书院，寄《城南书院杂咏》及《城南图》于朱熹。作品：城南杂咏二十首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　建风雩亭于岳麓书院对山。作品：与朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年9月</a>　建成书楼。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　除旧职，知静江府，经略安抚广南西路。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　作《邵州复旧学记》<div id='poem_1272804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邵州复旧学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272804")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272804'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272804'>庆历中，天子诏天下都邑皆得立学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272804_comment'></div>邵州去王畿数千里，于时亦为学以应诏旨，而学在牙城之中，左狱右庾，庳陋弗称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272804_comment'></div>治平四年，驾部员外郎、通判永州周侯敦颐来摄郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272804_comment'></div>始至，伏谒先圣祠下，起而悚然，乃度高明之地，迁于城之东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272804_comment'></div>及其成，帅士者行释菜之礼以落之，今祠刻具存，可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272804_comment'></div>惟侯唱明绝学于千载之下，学者宗之，所谓濂溪先生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272804_comment'></div>在当时之所建立，后之人所宜谨守，以时修治，而贻之无穷可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272804_comment'></div>顾今仅百有馀年，而其间兴坏之不常，甚至于徇寻常利便之说，徙就他所，甚失推崇先生长者流风遗泽之意，而于学校之教，所害亦已大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272804_comment'></div>乾道九年，知州事胡侯华公叹息其故，与学教授议所以复之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272804_comment'></div>转运判官、提举学事黄侯洧闻之，颇捐缗钱以相其事，于是即治平故基而加辟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272804_comment'></div>祠祭有庙，讲肄有堂，栖息有斋，前后楼阁翚飞相望，下至库庾庖湢无不备具，而民不知其费，不与其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272804_comment'></div>遣使来请记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272804_comment'></div>某以为，《春秋》之义，善复古者，是诚可书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272804_comment'></div>然尝考先王所以建学造士之本意，盖将使士者讲夫仁义礼智之彝，以明夫君臣、父子、兄弟、夫妇、朋友之伦，以之修身、齐家、治国、平天下，其事盖甚大矣，而为之则有其序，教之则有其方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272804_comment'></div>故必先使之从事于小学，习乎六艺之节，讲乎为弟、为子之职，而躬乎洒扫应对进退之事，周旋乎俎豆羽籥之间，优游乎弦歌诵读之际，有以固其肌肤之会、筋骸之束，齐其耳目，一其心志，所谓大学之道格物致知者，由是可以进焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272804_comment'></div>至于物格知至，而仁义礼知之彝得于其性，君臣、父子、兄弟、夫妇、朋友之伦皆以不乱，而修身、齐家、治国、平天下无不宜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272804_comment'></div>此先王之所以教而三代之所以治，后世不可以跂及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272804_comment'></div>后世之学校，朝夕所讲，不过缀缉文辞，以为规取利禄之计，亦与古之道大戾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272804_comment'></div>上之人所以教养成就之者，夫岂端为是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272804_comment'></div>今邵幸蒙诏旨，得立学宫，而周先生实经理其始，又幸而得复其旧于已废之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272804_comment'></div>士者游于其间，盍试思夫当时先生所以望于后人者，其亦如后之学校之所为乎，抑将以古之道而望之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272804_comment'></div>往取其遗书而读之，则亦可以见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272804_comment'></div>于是而相与讲明，以析夫义利之分，循古人小学、大学之序如前所云者，勉之而勿舍，则庶几为不负先生经始期望之意，而有以仰称上之人教养成就之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272804_comment'></div>今日之复是学，斯不为虚设矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272804_comment'></div>学故有二记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272804_comment'></div>其一治平五年湖北转运使孔侯延之之文，盖为周先生作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272804_comment'></div>其一绍兴二十三年武夷胡子宏之文，虽不详学之兴废，而开示学者为仁之方则甚明，皆足以传后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272804_comment'></div>某不敏，幸以浅陋之辞列于二记之次，实荣且愧云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272804_comment'></div>淳熙元年三月癸巳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1272804_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='68f57e4dacaf4235923475f93be3db3c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("68f57e4dacaf4235923475f93be3db3c");'><span id='68f57e4dacaf4235923475f93be3db3c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>，43岁</div><div id='68f57e4dacaf4235923475f93be3db3c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　秋，奉命作书，谕占城国王。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
永州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3f98b21898764ef7a7292cd83349a53a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3f98b21898764ef7a7292cd83349a53a");'><span id='3f98b21898764ef7a7292cd83349a53a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1155')">1150-1155年</a>，18-23岁</div><div id='3f98b21898764ef7a7292cd83349a53a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年9月</a>　随父至永州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1154')">1151-1154年</a>　侍亲家中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年10月</a>　作《悫斋铭》<div id='poem_1272869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>悫斋铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十五年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272869")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272869'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272869'>家君命枃以「悫」名其斋，而命栻铭以告之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272869_comment'></div>栻敬问所以为铭之意，盖取夫孔子曰「志必悫而后求智能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272869_comment'></div>退而深思，以为之铭：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1272869'>士或志近，辩给智巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272869_comment'></div>学之不知，其器则小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272869_comment'></div>天下之理，惟实为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272869_comment'></div>实不在外，当悫乎己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272869_comment'></div>不震不摇，物孰加之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272869_comment'></div>以此操行，谁曰不宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272869_comment'></div>古之君子，惟悫之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272869_comment'></div>不可小知，而可大受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272869_comment'></div>故以此事亲斯为孝，以此事君斯为忠，以此事兄斯为悌，交于朋友斯为信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272869_comment'></div>子其深思而不忒，维师乎悫，以令子之德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1272869_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8e0b1d41bb9248a98ad4d4668d0d707e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8e0b1d41bb9248a98ad4d4668d0d707e");'><span id='8e0b1d41bb9248a98ad4d4668d0d707e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1160')">1157-1160年</a>，25-28岁</div><div id='8e0b1d41bb9248a98ad4d4668d0d707e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1158')">1157-1158年</a>　侍亲家中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　邂逅零陵丞杨万里，为介绍于父亲张浚。<br /><a -----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='60640b663f0443079bd8c72c75cfac17_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("60640b663f0443079bd8c72c75cfac17");'><span id='60640b663f0443079bd8c72c75cfac17_link' DetailSwitch("5f9928822da548efbe6df0e2cc4c552f");'><span id='5f9928822da548efbe6df0e2cc4c552f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript:
