ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　应召入宫奏事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　见高宗于德寿宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年9月</a>　复被召入见，奉父命奏卢仲贤辱国无状，且奏仲贤不可不明正其罚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　复见高宗于德寿宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　见孝宗于东华门。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1ae698d10d75406f8c066b6fa406b518_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1ae698d10d75406f8c066b6fa406b518");'><span id='1ae698d10d75406f8c066b6fa406b518_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，37岁</div><div id='1ae698d10d75406f8c066b6fa406b518' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年12月25日</a>　以补郡临遣，得复见皇上，接连论奏。作品：答柳严州启。<div id='poem_1272439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答柳严州启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年12月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272439")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272439'>奉诏牧民，方待临川之次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272439_comment'></div>蒙恩易郡，更叨桐水之除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272439_comment'></div>自揆初心，敢忘素守！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272439_comment'></div>已上奉祠之请，辄辞乘传之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272439_comment'></div>岂不知在今此州，实拱行阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272439_comment'></div>仰云天之在望，知日月之可依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272439_comment'></div>地望既隆，民俗且简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272439_comment'></div>几席枕湖山之上，簿书杂鱼鸟之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272439_comment'></div>前瞻文正之风流，尚想子陵之节概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272439_comment'></div>叨逾过分，夫复何言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272439_comment'></div>然某方兹退伏于里闾，且欲从容于学问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272439_comment'></div>斯未能信，敢言轻试于治人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272439_comment'></div>道之难明，祗合静求于在己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272439_comment'></div>庶几有得，不辱其先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272439_comment'></div>日冀大君之仁，俯从小己之愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272439_comment'></div>岂谓山川之阻，忽勤鱼素之攽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272439_comment'></div>敢占芜辞，少叙鄙意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272439_comment'></div>恭惟知府朝议以德履之甚茂，全天才之有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272439_comment'></div>惟自处期忠厚之归，故所至以牧养为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272439_comment'></div>翱翔中外，益著声猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272439_comment'></div>咏《中和》之诗，已腾声于近服；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272439_comment'></div>陈《治安》之策，即趋对于明庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272439_comment'></div>某未谐先睹之期，徒负告新之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272439_comment'></div>敢借偃藩之乐，少留坐啸之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272439_comment'></div>秋律既深，霜飙愈厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272439_comment'></div>愿体眷毗之厚，益精调护之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272439_comment'></div>瞻颂之深，敷宣罔既！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272439_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1272439_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c037c12f554d41fab225a280aef80cda_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c037c12f554d41fab225a280aef80cda");'><span id='c037c12f554d41fab225a280aef80cda_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1171')">1170-1171年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='c037c12f554d41fab225a280aef80cda' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年闰5月17日</a>　自严州赴召。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年闰5月</a>　廷对。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年6月</a>　入见皇上，连次论奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　自省中归，读《西铭》作品：与朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年8月</a>　与吕祖谦同巷而居，相约共为夜课。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　与陈傅良论学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年2月</a>　开经筵，将《葛覃》篇，推广其事以进陈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年3月</a>　接连上疏，言张说不宜执政，面责丞相虞允文于朝堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年6月12日</a>　以论近习张说，被命出知袁州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年6月13日</a>　早晨出北关。<br class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545700'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545700'>芒鞋踏破万重山，五日淹留在此间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545700'>行客归来山下望，却疑身自九天还<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545700'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_545700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_545700'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_545700_0'>⑴ 以上《南岳酬唱集》　按：《南岳酬唱集》多有舛误，除以上五首外，尚有《自西园登山宿方广寺》等，视其内容，非朱熹所作。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_545700_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月16日</a>　自上封寺下福岩寺，作诗。作品：自上封下福岩道旁访李邺侯书堂山路榛合不可往矣。<div id='poem_112934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_112934' class='poemTitle </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_112934")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_112934_comment'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_113152_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月16日</a>　送别朱熹。作品：诗送朱元晦尊兄。<div id='poem_113328' id='poem_sentence_0_113328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113328'>顷登文石陛，忠言动宸旒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
湘潭
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e4a2883291a74c3a856bf6fdc02f0711_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e4a2883291a74c3a856bf6fdc02f0711");'><span id='e4a2883291a74c3a856bf6fdc02f0711_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1168')">1167-1168年</a>，35-36岁</div><div id='e4a2883291a74c3a856bf6fdc02f0711' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月</a>　过胡安国碧泉书堂。作品：过胡文定公碧泉书堂。<div id='poem_113300' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113300' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113300?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过胡文定公碧泉书堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113300")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_113300_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113300'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113300'>入门认溪碧，循流识深源。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113300'>念我昔此来，及今七寒暄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113300'>人事几更变，寒花故犹存。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113300'>堂堂武夷翁，道义世所尊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113300'>永袖霖雨手，琴书贲丘园。<div id='poem_sentence_4_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_113300'>当时经行地，尚想语笑温。<div id='poem_sentence_5_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_113300'>爱此亭下水，固若玻璃盆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_113300'>晴看浪花涌，静见潜鳞翻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_113300'>朝昏递日月，俯仰鉴乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_113300'>因之发深感，倚槛更忘言。<div id='poem_sentence_9_113300_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_113300'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_113300_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年4月</a>　记郴州学。作品：郴州学记。<div id='poem_1272805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272805?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郴州学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272805")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272805'>维三代之学，至周而大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272805_comment'></div>自天子之国都以及于乡党，莫不有学，使之朝夕优游于弦诵咏歌之中，而服习乎进退揖逊之节，则又申之以孝弟之义，为之冠昏丧祭之法，春秋释菜，与夫乡饮酒养老之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272805_comment'></div>其耳目手足肌肤之会、筋骸之束无不由于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272805_comment'></div>在上则司徒总其事，乐正崇其教，下而乡党亦莫不有师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272805_comment'></div>其教养之也密，故其成才也易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272805_comment'></div>士生斯时，藏修游息于其间，诵其言而知其味，玩其文而会其理，德业之进，日引月长，自宜然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272805_comment'></div>于是自乡论其行而升之司徒，司徒又论之而升之国庠，大乐正则察其成以告于王，定其论而官之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272805_comment'></div>其官之也，因其材之大小，盖有一居其官，至于终身不易者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272805_comment'></div>士修其身而已，非有求于君也，身修而君举之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272805_comment'></div>夫然，故礼义兴行，人才众多，风俗醇厚，至于斑白者不负戴于道路，而王道成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272805_comment'></div>国朝之学，视汉唐为盛，郡县皆得置学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272805_comment'></div>郡有教授以掌治之，部刺史、守令佐又得兼领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272805_comment'></div>其事亦既重矣，而士之居焉者大抵操笔习为文辞，以求应有司之程耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272805_comment'></div>嗟乎，是岂国家所望于多士之意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272805_comment'></div>虽教养之法疑若未尽复古，然为士者岂可不思士之所以为士者果为何事也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272805_comment'></div>郴故有学，迫于城隅，湫隘不治，知州事薛彦博、通判事卢𨓯、教授吴镒始议迁改，因得浮屠废宫，江山在前，高明爽垲，乃徙而一新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272805_comment'></div>郡之士相与劝率，以助资役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272805_comment'></div>甫踰时而迄成焉，来属某，愿有纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272805_comment'></div>某惟先王之于学，所以勤勤恳恳，若饮食起居之不可须臾离者，诚以正心、修身、齐家、治国以至于平天下，未有不须学而成者，实生民之大命，而王道之本原也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272805_comment'></div>然而学以何为要乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272805_comment'></div>孟子论三代之学，一言以蔽之，曰「皆所以明人伦」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272805_comment'></div>大哉言乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272805_comment'></div>人之大伦，天所叙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272805_comment'></div>降衷于民，谁独无是性哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272805_comment'></div>孩提之童，莫不知爱其亲，及其长也，莫不知敬其兄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272805_comment'></div>而夫妇、朋友之间，君臣之际，礼仪三百，威仪三千，无适而非性之所有者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272805_comment'></div>惟夫局于气禀，迁于物欲，而天理不明，是以处之不尽其道，以至于伤恩害义者有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272805_comment'></div>此先王之所以为忧，而为之学以教之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272805_comment'></div>然则学之所务，果何以外于人伦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272805_comment'></div>虽至于圣人，亦曰尽其性而为人伦之至耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272805_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272805_comment'></div>今之学者苟能立志尚友，讲论问辩，而于人伦之际审加察焉，敬守力行，勿舍勿夺，则良心可识，而天理自著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272805_comment'></div>驯是而进，益高益深，在家则孝弟雍睦之行兴，居乡则礼逊廉耻之俗成，一旦出而立朝，致君泽民，事业可大，则三代之风何远之有，岂不盛欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272805_comment'></div>又岂可不勉欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272805_comment'></div>学之成，实乾道四年春二月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1272805_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
建德
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='60b3ffa0f4854c55b3afd853c74b3d37_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("60b3ffa0f4854c55b3afd853c74b3d37");'><span id='60b3ffa0f4854c55b3afd853c74b3d37_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1170')">1169-1170年</a>，37-38岁</div><div id='60b3ffa0f4854c55b3afd853c74b3d37' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　虞允文屡次遣人致意，张栻不答。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　莅任严州知州，改州学之门南向。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　春，奏免丁盐钱绢，诏蠲其半。作品：与朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　为唐名相宋璟立孤高亭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　与吕祖谦、朱熹论胡宏《知言》作品：与朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　为吕祖谦所编次《阃范》作序。作品：阃范序。<div id='poem_1272682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>阃范序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272682")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272682'>天地奠位，而人生乎其中，其所以为人之道者，以其有父子之亲，长幼之序，夫妇之别，而又有君臣之义，朋友之交也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272682_comment'></div>是五者，天下所命，而非人之所能为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272682_comment'></div>有是性则具是道，初不为圣愚而损益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272682_comment'></div>圣人能尽其性，故为人伦之至，众人则有所蔽夺而沦失之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272682_comment'></div>虽然，亦岂不可反哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272682_comment'></div>圣人有教焉，所以化其欲而反其初也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272682_comment'></div>舜之命契曰：「敬敷五教，在宽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272682_comment'></div>宽云者，渐濡涵养之，使其所素有者自发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272682_comment'></div>而咎繇亦曰：「天叙有典，敕我五典五敦哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272682_comment'></div>曰敕云者，所以正其纲，而敦云者，所以厚其性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272682_comment'></div>降及三代，庠序之教尤详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272682_comment'></div>故孟子曰：「学则三代共之，皆所以明人伦也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272682_comment'></div>明云者，讲明之而使之识其理之所以然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272682_comment'></div>惟先王道行于家，而化浃乎天下，万事以正，万物以遂，气志交孚，而无不应焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272682_comment'></div>至于世衰道微之时，而流泽之在人心，不可以壅遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272682_comment'></div>故《诗》三百篇，发乎情，止乎礼义者，圣人犹有取云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272682_comment'></div>然则人之所以为圣贤，与夫圣贤之教人，舍是五者，其何以哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272682_comment'></div>东莱吕祖谦伯恭父为严陵教官，与其友取《易》、《春秋》、《书》、《诗》、《礼传》、《鲁论》、《孟子》，圣贤所以发明人伦之道见于父子兄弟夫妇之际者，悉笔之于编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272682_comment'></div>又泛考子史诸书，上下二千馀载间，凡可以示训者皆辑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272682_comment'></div>惟其事之可法而已，载者之失实有所不计也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272682_comment'></div>惟其长之可取而已，它为之未善有不暇问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272682_comment'></div>间日携所编以示某而讲订焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272682_comment'></div>未几而成，名以《阃范》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272682_comment'></div>某谓此书行于世，家当藏之，而人当学之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272682_comment'></div>家庭闺阃之内，乡里族党之间，随其见之深浅、味之短长，笃敬力行，皆足以有补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272682_comment'></div>然在学者则当由是而讲明之，以求识其理之所以然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272682_comment'></div>诚知是书所载，莫非吾分内事，而古之君子皆非有所为而为之，则其精微亲切，必有隐然自得于中者，虽欲舍是而不由，亦不可得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272682_comment'></div>书所登载未尽，伯恭尚继编云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1272682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　类集《论语》“仁”字，各为之说，撰成《洙泗言仁录》，并寄示朱熹。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年闰5月</a>　刊《太极通书》于严州学宫，又刊《二程遗书》作品：通书后跋。<div id='poem_1272702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通书后跋<span class='inlineComment2'>（乾道六年闰五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年闰5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272702")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272702'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272702'>濂溪周先生《通书》，友人朱熹元晦以《太极图》列于篇首，而题之曰《太极通书》，某刻于严陵学宫，以示多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272702_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272702_comment'></div>自圣学不明，语道者不睹夫大全，卑则割裂而无统，高则汗漫而不精，是以性命之说不参乎事物之际，而经世之务仅出乎私意小智之为，岂不可叹哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272702_comment'></div>惟先生生乎千有馀载之后，超然独得夫《大易》之传，所谓《太极图》乃其纲领也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272702_comment'></div>推明动静之一源，以见生化之不穷，天命流行之体无乎不在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272702_comment'></div>文理密察，本末该贯，非阐微极幽，莫能识其指归也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272702_comment'></div>然而学者若之何而可以进于是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272702_comment'></div>亦曰敬而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272702_comment'></div>诚能起居食息主一而不舍，则其德性之知，必有卓然不可掩于体察之际者，而后先生之蕴可得而穷，太极可得而识矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272702_comment'></div>乾道庚寅闰月谨题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1272702_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
桂林
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='55bbd32977a1497c87d2a6d0ac828d36_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("55bbd32977a1497c87d2a6d0ac828d36");'><span id='55bbd32977a1497c87d2a6d0ac828d36_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>，43岁</div><div id='55bbd32977a1497c87d2a6d0ac828d36' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年2月24日</a>　至桂林，改斋名曰“无倦”，作记书之座右。作品：无倦斋记。<div id='poem_1272832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>无倦斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年2月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272832")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272832'>广西经略使所治厅事之西偏，有斋直喜丰堂之后，方而虚明，于燕息为宜，旧以「缓带」名，予惧其肆也，更题曰「无倦」，且志其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272832_comment'></div>昔者洙泗之门，子张问政，夫子首告之以无倦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272832_comment'></div>及季路之请益，则又终之以无倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272832_comment'></div>是知为政始终之道，无越乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272832_comment'></div>夫难存而易怠者心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272832_comment'></div>吏者分天子之民而治焉，受天子之土而守焉，一日之间，所为酬酢事物者亦不一端矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272832_comment'></div>几微之所形，纪纲之所寓，常隐于所忽而坏于所因循，纤毫之不谨，而万绪之失其机，方寸之不存，而千里之受其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272832_comment'></div>又况欲动而物乘，意佚而形随，其所差缪复何可胜计，可不畏哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272832_comment'></div>于是知圣人无倦之意深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272832_comment'></div>师也穷乎高明，而惧其所践之未笃也，故使以居之无倦为本，而继以行之以忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272832_comment'></div>由也勇于进为，而惧其有所忽也，故既告以先之劳之，及其请益，则继以无倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272832_comment'></div>以二子而圣人所以勉之者如此，则在他人其所当从事抑可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272832_comment'></div>虽然，常人之情，往往始之谨而末之慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272832_comment'></div>守失于终，事废于久者，盖多矣，非敦笃乎敬者，其能日新而无斁哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272832_comment'></div>予于此惧，书于坐右以自警，并以告来者云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1272832_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年2月</a>　祭舜庙，举庳亭神及唐武照像，投入庙前江中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年2月</a>　作谕俗文。<div id='poem_1272434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272434' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谕俗文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272434")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272434_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272434'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272434'>权发遣静江军府事，当职到任，访闻管下旧来风俗不美事件，理合先行告谕下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272434'>一、访闻愚民无知，遇有灾病等事，妄听师巫等人邪说，辄归罪父祖坟墓不吉，发掘取棺，栖寄它处，谓之出祖，动经年岁，不得归土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272434_comment'></div>契勘在法，犯他人坟墓，刑禁甚重，岂有自己祖先既已归土，妄谓于己不利，自行发掘，于天理人情，岂不伤害？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272434_comment'></div>榜到日，如有出祖未归土者，仰限一月，各复收葬，过限不葬，及今后有犯上项事节，并许人陈告，依条施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272434_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1272434'>一、访闻愚民无知，丧葬之礼不遵法度，装迎之际务为华饰，墟墓之间，过为屋宇，及听僧人等诳诱，多作缘事，广办斋筵，竭产假贷，以侈靡相誇，不能办者往往停丧，不以时葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272434_comment'></div>曾不知丧葬之礼务在主于哀敬，随家力量，使亡者以时归土，便是孝顺，岂在侈靡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272434_comment'></div>无益亡者，有害风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272434_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1272434'>一、访闻婚姻之际，亦复僭度，以财相徇，以气相高，帷帐酒食，过为华靡，以至男女失时，淫辟之讼多往往由此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272434_comment'></div>曾不知为父母之道，要使男女及时，各有所归，婚姻结好，岂为财物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272434_comment'></div>其侈靡等事，一时之间徒足以欺眩乡闾无知之人，而在身在家，所损不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272434_comment'></div>若有不悛，当治其尤甚者，以正风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272434_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1272434'>一、访闻愚民无知，生子多不举，在于刑禁至重，前后官司，举行戒谕非不丁宁，往往习俗未能悛改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272434_comment'></div>人各有生，莫亲于父母儿女之爱，何忍至此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272434_comment'></div>男女虽多，它日岂不能相助营缉生计，宁有反患不给之理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272434_comment'></div>以利灭亲，悖逆天道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272434_comment'></div>如有不悛，许人告捉，支赏依条施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272434_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1272434'>一、访闻愚民无知，病不服药，妄听师巫淫祀谄祷，因循至死，反谓祈祷未至，曾不之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272434_comment'></div>甚至卧病在床，至亲不视，极害义理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272434_comment'></div>契勘疾病生于寒暑冲冒，饮食失时，自合问医用药治疗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272434_comment'></div>亲戚之间，当兴孝慈之心，相与照管，其邻里人等亦合时来存问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272434_comment'></div>至于师巫之说，皆无是理，只是撰造恐动，使人离析亲党，破损钱物，枉坏性命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272434_comment'></div>上件诳惑百姓之人，本府已出榜禁止捉押，决定依条重作施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272434_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1272434'>一、访闻乡落愚民诱引他人妻室，贩卖他处，谓之捲伴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272434_comment'></div>词讼到官，追治监锢，押往寻觅，缘此破荡者前后非一，不知惩戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272434_comment'></div>其捲伴之人，官司自合严行惩治外，亦缘细民往往不务安业，葺理农事，多往南州兴贩，逐锥刀之利，动经年岁不返乡闾，妻室无依，以至为他人捲伴前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272434_comment'></div>自今各仰依分安常，营生自守，保其家室，无致招悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272434_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1272434'>右，上件事理，并仰乡民反复思念，递相告谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272434_comment'></div>父老长上教敕子弟，共行遵依，以善风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272434_comment'></div>或致犯法，后悔难追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272434_comment'></div>各仰知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272434_comment'></div>淳熙二年三月日榜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1272434_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年6月</a>　率学子俯伏三先生祠前。作品：三先生祠记。<div id='poem_1272822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三先生祠记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272822")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272822'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272822'>淳熙二年，静江守臣张某即学宫明伦堂之旁立三先生祠，濂溪周先生在东序，明道程先生、伊川程先生在西序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272822_comment'></div>绘像既严，以六月壬子率学之士俯伏而告成，退则进而谂之曰：师道之不可不立也久矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272822_comment'></div>良才美质，何世无之，而后世之人才所以不古如者，以夫师道之不立故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272822_comment'></div>凡所谓为士者固曰以孔孟为宗，然而莫知所以自进于孔孟之门墙，则亦没世穷年，伥伥然如旅人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272822_comment'></div>幸而有先觉者出，得其传于千载之下，私淑诸人，使学者知夫儒学之真，求之有道，进之有序，以免于异端之归，去孔孟之世虽远，而与亲炙之者固亦何以相异，独非幸哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272822_comment'></div>是则秦汉以来师道之立，宜莫盛于今也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272822_comment'></div>而近世学者诚知所信慕者盖鲜，间有号为推尊，则又或窃虚声以自高，而不克践其实，顾反以为病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272822_comment'></div>是则师道虽在天下，而学者亦莫知其立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272822_comment'></div>桂之为州，僻处岭外，山拔而水清，士之秀美者夫岂乏人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272822_comment'></div>惟见闻之未广，而勉励之无从，故某之区区，首以立师道为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272822_comment'></div>继自今瞻三先生之在此祠也，其各起敬起慕，求其书而读之，味其言，考其行，讲论䌷绎，心存而身履，循之以进于孔孟之门墙，将见人才之作兴，与漓江为无穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272822_comment'></div>此某之所望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272822_comment'></div>且独不见濂溪先生之言乎，曰：「师道立则善人多，善人多则朝廷正而天下治」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272822_comment'></div>嗟乎，某之所望，又岂特于邦之士云哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272822_comment'></div>敢记而刻诸石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272822_comment'></div>后十日张栻记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1272822_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年7月</a>　斋戒，望奠于城观之上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年7月</a>　奏请与宪曹共究一路财赋，通融均济，为久远之计。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　奏改诸州息钱，并减阳朔、荔浦、修仁三县税米。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年7月</a>　率僚属祭虞帝庙，有书致朱熹，请作修虞帝庙碑文。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4a399d543dd744d4961a091d60eaf267_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a399d543dd744d4961a091d60eaf267");'><span id='4a399d543dd744d4961a091d60eaf267_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1178')">1175-1178年</a>，43-46岁</div><div id='4a399d543dd744d4961a091d60eaf267' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年8月</a>　作诗贻曾撙以劝学。作品：曾节夫罢官归旴江以小诗寄别。<div id='poem_113222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曾节夫罢官归旴江以小诗寄别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113222")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_113222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113222'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113222'>俗隘宁为异，言深敢自欺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113222_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113222'>如何幕中辩，翻作暗投疑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113222_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113222'>行李秋将半，家园菊正滋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113222_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113222'>反躬端得味，当复有馀师。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113222_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113222'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_113222_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　奏请推办本路保伍，饬下有司考定酌行，并奏乞选辟邕州提举巡检官，以抚洞丁。从之。作品：与曾节夫书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　奏改革马政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　率僚属祭尧山漓江二坛。作品：尧山漓江二坛记。<div id='poem_1272814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尧山漓江二坛记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272814")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272814'>古者诸侯各得祭其境内之山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272814_comment'></div>山川之所以为神灵者，以其气之所蒸，能出云雨，润泽群物，是故为之坛壝，立之祝史，设之牲币，所以致吾祷祀之实，而交孚乎隐显之际，诚之不可掩也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272814_comment'></div>后世固亦有山川之祠，而人其形，宇其地，则其失也久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272814_comment'></div>夫山峙而川流，是其形也，而人之也何居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272814_comment'></div>其气之流通，可以相接也，而宇之也何居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272814_comment'></div>无其理而强为之，虽百拜而祈，备物以飨，其有时而应也，亦偶然而已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272814_comment'></div>淳熙二年之春，某来守桂，按其图籍，览观其山川，所谓尧山者，蟠据于东，气象杰出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272814_comment'></div>环城之山，大抵皆石，而兹山独以壤，天将雨则云气先冒其颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272814_comment'></div>山之麓故有唐帝庙，山因以得名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272814_comment'></div>而漓江逶迤，自城之北转而东以达于南，清洁可鉴，其源发于兴安，与湘江同本而异派，故谓之漓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272814_comment'></div>而以水媲之，凡境内之水皆汇焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272814_comment'></div>以是知尧山、漓江为吾土之望，其馀莫能班也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272814_comment'></div>岁七月弥旬不雨，禾且告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272814_comment'></div>先一日斋戒，以夜漏未尽望奠于城观之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272814_comment'></div>曾未旋踵，雷电交集，一雨三日，均浃四境，邦人驩呼，穑以大稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272814_comment'></div>伏自念山川为吾土之望，而坛壝未立，祷祀无所，其何以率吾民严昭事之意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272814_comment'></div>用惕然不敢宁，乃俾临桂县尉范子之文度高明爽垲之地，得于城之北叠彩岩之后，隐然下临漓江，而江之外正与尧山相直，面势回环，表里呈露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272814_comment'></div>对筑二坛，以奉祀事，为屋三楹于坛之下，以备风雨，其外则绕以崇垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272814_comment'></div>踰时而告成，乃十有二月丁酉，率僚吏躬祭其上，以祈嗣岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272814_comment'></div>事毕裴徊，喟然叹息，退而述所以为坛之意，以告邦之人与来为政者，使知事神之义在此而不在彼，庶有以致其祷祀之实，且得以传之于无穷云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1272814_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　刻石𡼖《中庸集解》于桂林郡学宫。作品：跋《中庸集解》<div id='poem_1272701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋中庸集解</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272701")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272701'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272701'>右石𡼖子重所编《集解》两卷，某刻于桂林郡学宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272701_comment'></div>子重之编此书，尝从吾友朱熹元晦讲订，分章去取，皆有条次，元晦且尝为之序矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272701_comment'></div>桂林学官旧亦刻《中庸解》，而其间杂乱以他，惧其反误学者，于是漫去旧版，而更刻此书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272701_comment'></div>窃惟《中庸》一篇，圣贤之渊源也，体用隐显，成己成物备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272701_comment'></div>虽然，学者欲从事乎此，必知所从入而后可以驯致焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272701_comment'></div>其所从入奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272701_comment'></div>子思以「不睹不闻」之训著于篇首，又于篇终发明尚絅之义，且曰「君子之所不可及者，其惟人之所不见乎」，而推极夫笃恭之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272701_comment'></div>其示来世，可谓深切著明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272701_comment'></div>学者于此亦知所用其力哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272701_comment'></div>有以用其力，则于是书反复䌷绎，将日新而无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272701_comment'></div>不然，譬诸枵腹而观他人之食之美也，亦奚以益哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1272701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1272701'><span class='label'>按：</span>《南轩集》卷三三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一五○。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1272701_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　刻范仲淹帖于桂林郡斋。作品：跋范文正公帖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　与漕臣詹仪之协议，定盐法并官卖盐价，且条上之，皆蒙准行。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年6月</a>　刊司马光、张载、程颐三家婚丧祭礼于桂林郡学宫。作品：跋三家昏丧祭礼。<div id='poem_1272706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋三家昏丧祭礼</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272706")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272706'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272706'>右文正司马公、横渠张先生、伊川程先生《昏丧祭礼》，合为五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272706_comment'></div>窃惟道莫重乎人伦，教莫先乎礼，礼行则彝伦叙而人道立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272706_comment'></div>先王本天理，因人心而为之节文，其大体固根乎性命之际，而至于毫釐曲折之间，莫不各有精义存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272706_comment'></div>当是时，人由于其中，涵泳服习，敦庞淳固，盖有不期而然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272706_comment'></div>自先王之制日以缺坏，情文之不称，本末之失序，节乖而目疏，甚至于杂以异端之说，沦胥而入于夷，风俗之所以不厚，人才之所以不振，职是故欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272706_comment'></div>夫冠昏丧祭，人事之始终也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272706_comment'></div>冠礼之废久矣，未能遽复也，今姑即昏丧祭三者而论之，幸而有如三公之说，其可不尽心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272706_comment'></div>三公之使定，虽有异同，然至其推本先王之意，罢黜异端之说，是则未尝不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272706_comment'></div>司马氏盖已著言，若横渠、伊川二先生虽尝草定而未具，然所与门人讲论反复，其所发明深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272706_comment'></div>抑尝谓礼之兴废，学士大夫之责也，有能即是书探考而深思，深思而力行，宗族相亲，朋友相辅，安知风俗之美，不由是而作兴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272706_comment'></div>妄意可助圣时善俗之一端，于是刻于桂林郡之学宫云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272706_comment'></div>淳熙三年六月甲戌朔旦。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1272706'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1272706_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　刻成虞帝庙摩崖。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　摄宪曹两台，决遣一路滞狱苛征。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　删改《孟子说》作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　擒巨盗，奏请严保伍之令，信其赏罚，上皆许之。作品：与曾节夫书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年2月</a>　新修陶唐帝庙成，奏闻，并率僚属祭之。作品：谒陶唐帝庙词。<div id='poem_113377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒陶唐帝庙词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113377")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_113377_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_113377'>宋淳熙四年，静江守臣张某既新陶唐帝祠，以二月甲子率官属祗谒祠下，再拜稽首，退而歌曰：</div><div id='poem_preface_113377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113377'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113377'>溪交流兮谷幽，山作屏兮层丘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113377'>木偃蹇兮枝相樛，皇胡为兮于此留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113377'>蔼冠佩兮充庭，洁芳馨兮载陈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113377'>纯衣兮在御，东风吹兮物为春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113377'>皇之仁兮其天，四时叙兮何言。<div id='poem_sentence_4_113377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_113377'>出门兮四顾，渺宇宙兮茫然。<div id='poem_sentence_5_113377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_113377'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_113377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_113377'><span class='label'>按：</span>《南轩集》卷一。又见《芦浦笔记》卷四，《南宋文范》卷三。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_113377_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年2月16日</a>　奉诏劝农于郊。作品：淳熙四年二月既望静江守臣张某奉诏劝农于郊乃作熙熙阳春之诗二十四章章四句以示父老俾告于其乡之人而歌之。<div id='poem_546301' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546301' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546301?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淳熙四年二月既望静江守臣张某奉诏劝农于郊乃作熙熙阳春之诗二十四章章四句以示父老俾告于其乡之人而歌之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年2月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_546301")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546301_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546301'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546301'>熙熙阳春，既发既舒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546301'>翼翼南亩，是展是图。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_1_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546301'>嗟尔农夫，各敬乃事。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546301'>往利尔器，诫尔妇子。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_3_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546301'>惟生在勤，勤则及时。<div id='poem_sentence_4_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_546301'>惟时之趋，时不尔违。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_5_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_546301'>祁祁甘雨，膏我下土。<div id='poem_sentence_6_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_546301'>习习谷风，和泽乃普。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_7_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_546301'>往即尔耕，惟力之深。<div id='poem_sentence_8_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_546301'>往莳尔苗，勿倦其耘。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_9_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_546301'>于日于夕，自遂自达。<div id='poem_sentence_10_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_546301'>尔心勿忘，彼生孰遏。<span class='charType'>（六章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_11_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_546301'>惟天之心，矜我下民。<div id='poem_sentence_12_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_546301'>民不违天，使尔有成。<span class='charType'>（七章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_13_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_546301'>既穟既实，既坚既好。<div id='poem_sentence_14_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_546301'>尔穫既周，先养尔老。<span class='charType'>（八章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_15_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_546301'>保尔家室，抚尔幼稚。<div id='poem_sentence_16_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_546301'>既迄有年，复思嗣岁。<span class='charType'>（九章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_17_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_546301'>嗟尔父老，其训其诫。<div id='poem_sentence_18_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_546301'>俾务于本，惟土物爱。<span class='charType'>（十章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_19_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_546301'>不念其本，则越其思。<div id='poem_sentence_20_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_546301'>所思既越，害斯百罹。<span class='charType'>（十一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_21_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_546301'>嗟尔父老，其告其喻。<div id='poem_sentence_22_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_546301'>尔之有生，君实覆汝。<span class='charType'>（十二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_23_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_546301'>尊君亲上，其笃勿忘。<div id='poem_sentence_24_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_546301'>小心畏忌，率于宪章。<span class='charType'>（十三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_25_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_546301'>嗟尔父老，教之孝悌。<div id='poem_sentence_26_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_546301'>孰无父母，与其同气。<span class='charType'>（十四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_27_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_546301'>反于尔心，孰无爱敬。<div id='poem_sentence_28_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_546301'>即是而推，乌往不顺。<span class='charType'>（十五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_29_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_546301'>嗟尔父老，勿替谆谆。<div id='poem_sentence_30_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_546301'>其未率从，警厉其身。<span class='charType'>（十六章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_31_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_546301'>告以祸患，其使知惧。<div id='poem_sentence_32_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_546301'>无俾蹉跌，以陷罪罟。<span class='charType'>（十七章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_33_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_546301'>惟国之法，烨烨其垂。<div id='poem_sentence_34_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_546301'>使尔知避，岂欲尔施。<span class='charType'>（十八章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_35_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_546301'>尔或自陷，予疚予恫。<div id='poem_sentence_36_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_546301'>曷使予怀，寘于尔衷。<span class='charType'>（十九章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_37_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_546301'>于赫圣主，敷德流泽。<div id='poem_sentence_38_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_546301'>布宣弗勤，时予之责。<span class='charType'>（二十章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_39_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_546301'>咨尔父老，助予念兹。<div id='poem_sentence_40_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_546301'>岂予之助，报国是宜。<span class='charType'>（二十一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_41_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_546301'>粤以今日，劝相于郊。<div id='poem_sentence_42_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_546301'>乃作此诗，以懋尔劳。<span class='charType'>（二十二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_43_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_546301'>咨尔父老，尚演厥义。<div id='poem_sentence_44_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_546301'>其讽其歌，于乡于里。<span class='charType'>（二十三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_45_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_546301'>俾一其心，服我训言。<div id='poem_sentence_46_546301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_546301'>击鼓坎坎，自古有年<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《南轩先生文集》卷三）</span>。<span class='charType'>（二十四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_47_546301_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_546301'></div><div id='poem_sentence_48_546301_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　特转承事郎，进直宝文阁。二月知静江府任满，再任。作品：进职因任谢表。<div id='poem_1272410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进职因任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272410")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272410'>内閤分华，进其寓直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272410_comment'></div>介藩因任，锡以赞书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272410_comment'></div>既莫遂于终辞，凛不知夫所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272410_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272410_comment'></div>伏念臣昨承人乏，来守岭隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272410_comment'></div>忽坐阅于两秋，亦既殚于五技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272410_comment'></div>所赖旁流之惠泽，故兹少息于疲氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272410_comment'></div>吏于其间，谴因以免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272410_comment'></div>敢希误宠，何有微劳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272410_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下以大有为之资，行不忍人之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272410_comment'></div>远迩一视，真传太上之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272410_comment'></div>赏罚至公，悉听国人之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272410_comment'></div>惟臣不敏，曷称所蒙！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272410_comment'></div>况闻前哲之言，多畏居官之久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272410_comment'></div>非人情狃习之为虑，实己志怠忽之难防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272410_comment'></div>其几弛于方寸之间，则害及于一路之广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272410_comment'></div>返复以念，经营莫宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272410_comment'></div>敢不履薄临深，益思谨于侯度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272410_comment'></div>庶几积铢累寸，或不玷于皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272410_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1272410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年6月</a>　刻陈瓘《责沈》于桂林学宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　寄《癸巳论语说》于朱熹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年8月</a>　妻宇文安人卒，子焯护丧归葬长沙。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年11月</a>　新修静江府学成，命其属下具图与书，使人于武夷山间谒朱熹。作品：静江府学记。<div id='poem_1272802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>静江府学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道六年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272802")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272802'>国朝学校遍天下，秦汉以来所未见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272802_comment'></div>桂林之学，自唐大历中观察使李昌夔经始于郊，而熙宁中徙于郡城东南隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272802_comment'></div>乾道二年，知府事张侯维又以其地堙陋，更相爽垲，得浮屠废宫，实故始安郡治，请于朝而迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272802_comment'></div>侯以书来曰：「愿有以告于桂之士」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272802_comment'></div>某惟古人所以从事于学者其果何所为而然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272802_comment'></div>天之生斯人也，则有常性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272802_comment'></div>人之立于天地之间也，则有常事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272802_comment'></div>在身有一身之事，在家有一家之事，在国有一国之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272802_comment'></div>其事也非人之所能为也，性之所有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272802_comment'></div>弗胜其事则为弗有其性，弗有其性则为弗克若天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272802_comment'></div>克保其性而不悖其事，所以顺乎天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272802_comment'></div>然则舍讲学其能之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272802_comment'></div>凡天下之事皆人之所当为，君臣、父子、兄弟、夫妇、朋友之际，人事之大者也，以至于视听言动、周旋食息，至纤至悉，何莫非事者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272802_comment'></div>一事之不贯，则天性以之陷溺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272802_comment'></div>然则讲学其可不汲汲乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272802_comment'></div>学所以明万事而奉天职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272802_comment'></div>虽然，事有其理而著于吾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272802_comment'></div>心也者，万事之宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272802_comment'></div>惟人放其良心，故事失其统纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272802_comment'></div>学也者，所以收其放而存其良也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272802_comment'></div>夏葛而冬裘，饥食而渴饮，理之所固存，而事之所当然者，凡吾于万事皆见其若是也，而后为当其可学者求乎此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272802_comment'></div>尝窃怪今世之学者其所从事往往异乎是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272802_comment'></div>鼓箧入学，抑亦思吾所谓学者果何事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272802_comment'></div>圣人之立教者果何在乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272802_comment'></div>而朝廷建学，群聚而教养者又果何为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272802_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272802_comment'></div>此独未之思而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272802_comment'></div>使其知所思，则必竦然动于中，而其朝夕所接，君臣、父子、兄弟、夫妇、朋友之际，视听言动之间，必有不得而遁者，庶乎可以知入德之门矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272802_comment'></div>某也不敏，何足以启告于人，辱侯盛意，勉为之书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1272802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1272802'><span class='label'>按：</span>《南轩集》卷九。又见《五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一○五，万历《广西志》卷三六，《古今图书集成》选举典卷二一、职方典卷一四○四。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1272802_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　丐祠，不获命，再辞。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　改正《论语说》作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　论李周翰《原说》之弊。作品：与吕季克书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年3月</a>　不赴史浩之荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　请诸邑有行义士人居学舍中。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　改革岭外风俗，执拘不奔父丧之浮屠以付其家。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年5月1日</a>　除秘阁修撰。作品：谢除秘阁修撰表。<div id='poem_1272411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除秘阁修撰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272411")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272411'>臣某言：先在广西任日，伏蒙圣恩除臣秘阁修撰，寻具辞免，奉圣旨不允，已祗受诰命者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272411_comment'></div>奉藩何补，坐费三年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272411_comment'></div>进律之褒，乃蒙再命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272411_comment'></div>控忱辞而莫获，拊小己以增羞<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272411_comment'></div>伏念臣钝质无堪，孤踪难植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272411_comment'></div>备保鄣于远服，凛危惧之百怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272411_comment'></div>惟仰恃于圣明，勉自殚其心力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272411_comment'></div>班超之策但守于平平，阳城之书固甘于下下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272411_comment'></div>岂期睿奖，荐赐宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272411_comment'></div>俯矜尘坌之馀生，俾隶蓬莱之高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272411_comment'></div>超踰若此，报称谓何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272411_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下器使群才，光被四表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272411_comment'></div>顾未忘于簪履之旧，尚念黯愚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272411_comment'></div>将示劝于牧圉之臣，姑从隗始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272411_comment'></div>荣踰华衮，愧甚循墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272411_comment'></div>臣敢不勉务朴忠，仰承德意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272411_comment'></div>始终一节，期不负于素怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272411_comment'></div>驱驰四方，敢或惮于烦使！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1272411_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　子焯病故，力请出广，遂除湖北路转运副使，改知江陵府，安抚本路。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年7月</a>　荐吴猎于刘焞，移使湖北，所至游历山川，在舟读书，修改《孟子说》作品：静江归舟中读书。<div id='poem_113399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>静江归舟中读书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113399")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_113399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113399'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113399'>南风驾小雨，群山净如沐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113399'>吾归及新凉，所历慰心目。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113399'>轧轧柔橹鸣，卧见山起伏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113399'>推枕意悠然，还取我书读。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113399'>平生领解处，于焉更三复。<div id='poem_sentence_4_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_113399'>老矣百念疏，但欲斯境熟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_113399'>向来五岭游，日力半吏牍。<div id='poem_sentence_6_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_113399'>小心了官事，终觉愧茕独。<div id='poem_sentence_7_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_113399'>世路自险夷，人情费追逐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_113399'>翩翩孤飞翼，息荫望林麓。<div id='poem_sentence_9_113399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_113399'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_113399_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宜春
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fa00d57746484de79c22ff2edfc669fe_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fa00d57746484de79c22ff2edfc669fe");'><span id='fa00d57746484de79c22ff2edfc669fe_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>，46岁</div><div id='fa00d57746484de79c22ff2edfc669fe' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年8月</a>　过其弟张枃于宜春，应州学教授李中等人所请，作《袁州学记》<div id='poem_1272803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>袁州学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙五年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272803")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272803'>淳熙五年秋八月，某来宜春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272803_comment'></div>至之明日，州学教授李中与州之士合辞来言：「宜春之学，自皇祐中太守祖无择实始为之，今百有二十五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272803_comment'></div>中更兵革，废而复兴，惟是庳陋弗克称，至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272803_comment'></div>守乃慨然按寻旧规，首辟讲肄之堂，立稽古阁于堂上，生师之舍皆撤而一新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272803_comment'></div>将告成，而君侯适来，敢请记以诏多士」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272803_comment'></div>某谢不敏，则请益坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272803_comment'></div>乃进而告之曰：先王所以建学造士之意，亦尝考之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272803_comment'></div>惟民之生，其典有五，君臣、父子、兄弟、夫妇、朋友是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272803_comment'></div>而其德有四，仁、义、礼、智是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272803_comment'></div>人能充其德之所固有，以率夫典之所当然，则必无力不足之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272803_comment'></div>惟人之不能是也，故圣人使之学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272803_comment'></div>自唐虞以来，固莫不以是教矣，至于三代之世，立教人之所，设官以董莅之，而其法益加详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272803_comment'></div>然其所以为教则一道耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272803_comment'></div>故曰：「学则三代共之，皆所以明人伦也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272803_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272803_comment'></div>人伦之在天下，不可一日废，废则国随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272803_comment'></div>然则有国者之于学，其可一日而忽哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272803_comment'></div>皇朝列圣相承，留意教养，所以望于多士甚厚，三代而下言学校之盛，未有若此时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272803_comment'></div>然则教于斯，学于斯者，其可不深考先王建学造士之本意而勉之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272803_comment'></div>惟四德之在人，各具于其性，人病不能求之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272803_comment'></div>求之之方，载于孔孟之书，备有科级，惟致其知而后可以有明，惟力其行而后可以有至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272803_comment'></div>孝弟之行，始乎闺门而形于乡党；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272803_comment'></div>忠爱之实，见于事君而推以泽民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272803_comment'></div>是则无负于国家之教养，而三代之士风亦不越是而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272803_comment'></div>嗟乎，可不勉哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272803_comment'></div>于是书以为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272803_comment'></div>今守名枃，实某之弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272803_comment'></div>是月庚戌记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1272803_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
澧县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='645a026eb4374ee1a7aacc1cf58bd4f8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("645a026eb4374ee1a7aacc1cf58bd4f8");'><span id='645a026eb4374ee1a7aacc1cf58bd4f8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>，46岁</div><div id='645a026eb4374ee1a7aacc1cf58bd4f8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　过澧州，澧州士子十数人执文书郊迎，举郡守刘某政绩。张栻还其文书，跃马而去。<br /></div>

-----title
江陵
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a7f5951da1784fccb223a9d0432d94b3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a7f5951da1784fccb223a9d0432d94b3");'><span id='a7f5951da1784fccb223a9d0432d94b3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1180')">1178-1180年</a>，46-48岁</div><div id='a7f5951da1784fccb223a9d0432d94b3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　到任，严缉捕之令，整顿军政。作品：答朱元晦书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　应道州郡守赵汝谊之请，作《道州重建濂溪周先生祠堂记》<div id='poem_1272816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道州重建濂溪周先生祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272816")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272816'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272816'>宋有天下，明圣相继，承平日久，元气胥会，至昭陵之世盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272816_comment'></div>宗工钜儒，磊落相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272816_comment'></div>于是时，濂溪先生实出于舂陵焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272816_comment'></div>先生姓周字茂叔，晚筑庐山之下，以濂名其溪，故世称为濂溪先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272816_comment'></div>舂陵之人言曰：濂溪，吾乡之里名也，先生世家其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272816_comment'></div>及寓于他邦，而不忘其所自生，故亦以是名溪，而世或未知之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272816_comment'></div>惟先生仕不大显于时，其泽不得究施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272816_comment'></div>然世之学者考论师友渊源，以孔孟之遗意复明于千载之下，实自先生发其端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272816_comment'></div>由是推之，则先生之泽，其何有穷哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272816_comment'></div>盖自孔孟没，而其微言仅存于简编，更秦火之馀，汉世儒者号为穷经学古，不过求于训诂章句之间，其于文义不能无时有所益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272816_comment'></div>然大本之不究，圣贤之心郁而不章，而又有颛从事于文辞者，其去古益以远，经生、文士自岐为二途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272816_comment'></div>及夫措之当世，施于事为，则又出于功利之末，智力之所营，若无所与于书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272816_comment'></div>于是有异端者乘间而入，横流于中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272816_comment'></div>儒而言道德性命者，不入于老，则入于释，间有希世杰出之贤，攘臂排之，而其为说复未足以尽吾儒之指归，故不足以抑其澜，而或反以激其势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272816_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272816_comment'></div>言学而莫适其序，言治而不本于学，言道德性命而流入于虚诞，吾儒之学其果如是乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272816_comment'></div>陵夷至此，亦云极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272816_comment'></div>及吾先生起于远方，乃超然有所自得于其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272816_comment'></div>本乎《易》之太极、《中庸》之诚，以极乎天地万物之变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272816_comment'></div>其教人使之志伊尹之志，学颜子之学，推之于治，先王之礼乐刑政可举而行，如指诸掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272816_comment'></div>于是河南二程先生兄弟从而得其说，推明究极之，广大精微，殆无馀蕴，学者始知夫孔孟之所以教，盖在此而不在乎他，学可以至于圣，治不可以不本于学，而道德性命初不外乎日用之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272816_comment'></div>其于致知力行，具有条理，而诐淫邪遁之说皆无以自隐，可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272816_comment'></div>然则先生发端之功，顾不大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272816_comment'></div>舂陵之学旧有先生祠，实绍兴某年向侯子忞所建，至于今淳熙五年，赵侯汝谊以其地之狭也，下车之始，即议更度之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272816_comment'></div>为堂四楹，并二程先生之像列于其中，规模周密，称其尊事之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272816_comment'></div>既成，使来谒记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272816_comment'></div>某谓先生之祠，凡学皆当有之，岂惟舂陵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272816_comment'></div>特在舂陵尤所当先者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272816_comment'></div>赵侯兹举知急务矣，故为之论述如此，以告后之人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1272816_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年1月</a>　楚望二坛成，率僚属以告。作品：楚望记。<div id='poem_1272815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272815?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楚望记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙六年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272815")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272815_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272815'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272815'>礼，诸侯望祭其境内之山川，必有坛壝以为岁时祈报之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272815_comment'></div>今之为郡，古诸侯国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272815_comment'></div>江陵据旧楚一都会，其山虽去郡为远，然迤逦联络，以属于当阳巫峡之间，有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272815_comment'></div>而其浸则有如蜀江波涛吐吞，㳽亘千里，长吏所当率民敬事弗怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272815_comment'></div>而望祭之地乃或有阙，始度寸金堤之会，平旷爽垲，爰筑二坛，既高既坚，绕以周墙，扁曰「楚望」，盖取《传》所谓「江汉沮漳，楚之望也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272815_comment'></div>于其成，率僚属以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272815_comment'></div>惟神之灵，佑此下土，时其雨旸，茂乃嘉生，使永无水旱厉疫之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272815_comment'></div>惟吏与民各端乃心，以承以引，无替于厥初，无使非鬼得以紊我常祀，神人相保，终古曷穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272815_comment'></div>遂书以贻来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272815_comment'></div>淳熙六年正月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1272815_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年2月</a>　经行郡圃，作《后杞菊赋》<div id='poem_1272405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后杞菊赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272405")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272405'>张子为江陵之数月，时方中春，草木敷荣，经行郡圃，意有所欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272405_comment'></div>非花柳之是问，眷杞菊之青青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272405_comment'></div>爰命采掇，付之庖人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272405_comment'></div>汲清泉以细烹，屏五味而不亲，甘脆可口，蔚其芳馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272405_comment'></div>盖日为之加饭，而它物几不足以前陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272405_comment'></div>饭已扪腹，得意讴吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272405_comment'></div>客有问者曰：「异哉，先生之嗜此也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272405_comment'></div>昔坡公之在胶西，值党禁之方兴，叹斋厨之萧条，乃揽乎草木之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272405_comment'></div>今先生当无事之世，据方伯之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272405_comment'></div>校吏奔走，颐指如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272405_comment'></div>广厦延宾，毬场享士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272405_comment'></div>清酒百壶，鼎臑俎胾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272405_comment'></div>宰夫奏刀，各献其技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272405_comment'></div>顾无求而弗获，虽醉饱其何忌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272405_comment'></div>而乃乐从夫野人之餐，岂亦下取乎葑菲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272405_comment'></div>不然，得无近于矫激，有同于脱粟布被者乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272405_comment'></div>张子笑而应之曰：「天壤之间，孰为正味？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272405_comment'></div>厚或腊毒，淡乃其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272405_comment'></div>猩唇豹胎，徒取诡异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272405_comment'></div>山鲜海错，纷纠莫计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272405_comment'></div>苟滋味之或偏，在六府而成赘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272405_comment'></div>极口腹之所欲，初何出乎一美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272405_comment'></div>惟杞与菊，中和所萃，微劲不苦，滑甘靡滞，非若他蔬，善呕走水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272405_comment'></div>既瞭目而安神，复沃烦而荡秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272405_comment'></div>验南阳与西河，又颓龄之可制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272405_comment'></div>此其为功，曷可殚纪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272405_comment'></div>况于膏粱之习，贫贱则废；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272405_comment'></div>隽永之求，不得则恚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272405_comment'></div>兹随寓之必有，虽约居而足恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272405_comment'></div>殆将与之终身，又可贻夫同志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272405_comment'></div>子独不见吾纳湖之阴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272405_comment'></div>雪消壤肥，其茸萎蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272405_comment'></div>与子婆娑，薄言掇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272405_comment'></div>石铫瓦碗，啜汁咀齑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272405_comment'></div>高论唐虞，咏歌《书》《诗》！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272405_comment'></div>微斯物，孰同先生之归」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1272405_comment'></div>于是相属而歌，殆日晏以忘饥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1272405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　诏与诸司议募弓弩手事，张栻为去其病民罔上者数条，诏皆施行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　答陆九龄书，论学。作品：答陆子寿书。<div id='poem_1272597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答陆子寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_1272597")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272597'>某闻昆仲之贤有年矣，近岁得之为尤详，每怀愿见，以共讲益，渺然相望而未克遂，向往可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272597_comment'></div>忽辱枉教，三复辞义，有感于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272597_comment'></div>第惟孤陋，不足以当盛意也，然而不敢以虚来贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272597_comment'></div>讲学不可以不精也，毫釐之差，则其弊有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272597_comment'></div>故夫专于考索，则有遗本溺心之患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272597_comment'></div>而骛于高远，则有躐等凭虚之忧，二者皆其弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272597_comment'></div>考圣人之教人，固不越乎致知力行之大端，患在人不知所用力耳，莫非致知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272597_comment'></div>日用之间，事之所遇，物之所触，思之所起，以至于读书考古，苟知所用力，则莫非吾格物之妙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272597_comment'></div>其为力行也，岂但见于孝悌忠信之所发，形于事而后为行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272597_comment'></div>自息养瞬存以至于三千三百之间，皆合内外之实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272597_comment'></div>行之力则知愈进，知之深则行愈达，区区诚有见乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272597_comment'></div>如笺注、诂训，学者虽不可使之溺乎此，又不可使之忽乎此，要当昭示以用工之实，而无忽乎细微之间，使之免溺心之病，而无躐等之失，涵濡浸渍，知所用力，则莫非实事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272597_comment'></div>凡左右之言，皆道其用力之实也，故乐以复焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272597_comment'></div>圣上聪明不世出，真难逢之会，所恨臣下未有以仰称明意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272597_comment'></div>大抵后世致君泽民之事业不大见于天下者，皆吾儒讲学不精之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272597_comment'></div>故区区每愿从世之贤者相与切磋究之，而盛意之辱，欣幸至于再三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272597_comment'></div>元晦卓然特立，真金石之友也，然作别十馀年矣，书问往来，终岂若会面之得尽其底里哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272597_comment'></div>伯恭一病，终未全复，深可念，向来亦坐枉费心思处多耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272597_comment'></div>心之精微，书莫能究，布复草草，正惟亮之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1272597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　赋诗寄朱熹。作品：庐山有胜处曰卧龙南康朱使君始筑茅绘诸葛武侯像于其中以书属予赋诗寄题此篇。<div id='poem_113315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山有胜处曰卧龙南康朱使君始筑茅绘诸葛武侯像于其中以书属予赋诗寄题此篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113315")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_113315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113315'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113315'>庐山仙灵宅，佳处固非一。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113315'>颇闻卧龙胜，幽深谅难匹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113315'>悬瀑泻琮琤，石壁两崒嵂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113315'>草木被光辉，波澜动回没。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113315'>今年朱使君，下马恍若失。<div id='poem_sentence_4_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_113315'>徘徊领妙趣，指点筑茅室。<div id='poem_sentence_5_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_113315'>为爱卧龙名，英姿慨超轶。<div id='poem_sentence_6_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_113315'>于焉俨绘事，长风起萧瑟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_113315'>髣髴梁父吟，尚想翁抱膝。<div id='poem_sentence_8_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_113315'>惨澹风云会，飘忽日月疾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_113315'>独存经世心，千载讵可汩。<div id='poem_sentence_10_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_113315'>褰裳欲从之，云涛渺寒日。<div id='poem_sentence_11_113315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_113315'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_113315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年9月9日</a>　出郊二十里，与宾佐登龙山。作品：重九日与宾佐登龙山。<div id='poem_113203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_113203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/113203?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重九日与宾佐登龙山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25690, "南宋", "张栻", "poem_title_113203")'>张栻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_113203_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_113203'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_113203'>晓风猎猎笛横秋，泽国名山九日游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_113203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_113203'>万里烟云归老眼，千年形势接中州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_113203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_113203'>丘原到处堪怀古，萸菊随时岂解愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_113203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_113203'>此日此心谁共领，朝宗江汉自东流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_113203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_113203'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_113203_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　李焘知常德府，奏乞度田立额，事下诸司，张栻韪其议，连名具奏，上从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　斩奸民出塞为盗者数人，缚亡奴归之北。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年11月</a>　建成曲江楼，有书请朱熹作记。作品：答朱元晦秘书书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　奏劾信阳守刘大辨，不报，自以不得其职，求去。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年11月</a>　生病，误服转下之药，遂至虚损。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年1月</a>　病重，屡次乞求免职，不许，乃以病请。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　自作遗表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年2月2日</a>　病故于江陵府舍。<br /></div>
